# Displayvideo_api Service



**Resources**: 144

---

## Resources


### Advertiser

Creates a new advertiser. Returns the newly created advertiser if successful. This method can take up to 180 seconds to complete.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser. Assigned by the system. |
| `creative_config` | String |  | Required. Creative related settings of the advertiser. |
| `prisma_enabled` | bool |  | Whether integration with Mediaocean (Prisma) is enabled. By enabling this, you agree to the following: On behalf of my company, I authorize Mediaocean (Prisma) to send budget segment plans to Google, and I authorize Google to send corresponding reporting and invoices from DV360 to Mediaocean for the purposes of budget planning, billing, and reconciliation for this advertiser. |
| `serving_config` | String |  | Targeting settings related to ad serving of the advertiser. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not insertion orders and line items of the advertiser can spend their budgets and bid on inventory. * Accepted values are `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`, `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` and `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`. * If set to `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`, the advertiser will be deleted 30 days from when it was first scheduled for deletion. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the advertiser was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `integration_details` | String |  | Integration details of the advertiser. Only integrationCode is currently applicable to advertiser. Other fields of IntegrationDetails are not supported and will be ignored if provided. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the advertiser. |
| `general_config` | String |  | Required. General settings of the advertiser. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the advertiser. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `ad_server_config` | String |  | Required. Immutable. Ad server related settings of the advertiser. |
| `data_access_config` | String |  | Settings that control how advertiser data may be accessed. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that the advertiser belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser. Assigned by the system. |
| `creative_config` | String | Required. Creative related settings of the advertiser. |
| `prisma_enabled` | bool | Whether integration with Mediaocean (Prisma) is enabled. By enabling this, you agree to the following: On behalf of my company, I authorize Mediaocean (Prisma) to send budget segment plans to Google, and I authorize Google to send corresponding reporting and invoices from DV360 to Mediaocean for the purposes of budget planning, billing, and reconciliation for this advertiser. |
| `serving_config` | String | Targeting settings related to ad serving of the advertiser. |
| `entity_status` | String | Required. Controls whether or not insertion orders and line items of the advertiser can spend their budgets and bid on inventory. * Accepted values are `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`, `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` and `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`. * If set to `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`, the advertiser will be deleted 30 days from when it was first scheduled for deletion. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the advertiser was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `integration_details` | String | Integration details of the advertiser. Only integrationCode is currently applicable to advertiser. Other fields of IntegrationDetails are not supported and will be ignored if provided. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the advertiser. |
| `general_config` | String | Required. General settings of the advertiser. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the advertiser. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `ad_server_config` | String | Required. Immutable. Ad server related settings of the advertiser. |
| `data_access_config` | String | Settings that control how advertiser data may be accessed. |
| `partner_id` | String | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that the advertiser belongs to. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create advertiser
advertiser = provider.displayvideo_api.Advertiser {
}

# Access advertiser outputs
advertiser_id = advertiser.id
advertiser_advertiser_id = advertiser.advertiser_id
advertiser_creative_config = advertiser.creative_config
advertiser_prisma_enabled = advertiser.prisma_enabled
advertiser_serving_config = advertiser.serving_config
advertiser_entity_status = advertiser.entity_status
advertiser_update_time = advertiser.update_time
advertiser_integration_details = advertiser.integration_details
advertiser_name = advertiser.name
advertiser_general_config = advertiser.general_config
advertiser_display_name = advertiser.display_name
advertiser_ad_server_config = advertiser.ad_server_config
advertiser_data_access_config = advertiser.data_access_config
advertiser_partner_id = advertiser.partner_id
```

---


### Floodlight_group

Gets a Floodlight group.

**Operations**: ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `web_tag_type` | String |  | Required. The web tag type enabled for the Floodlight group. |
| `active_view_config` | String |  | The Active View video viewability metric configuration for the Floodlight group. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |
| `lookback_window` | String |  | Required. The lookback window for the Floodlight group. Both click_days and impression_days are required. Acceptable values for both are `0` to `90`, inclusive. |
| `custom_variables` | HashMap<String, String> |  | User-defined custom variables owned by the Floodlight group. Use custom Floodlight variables to create reporting data that is tailored to your unique business needs. Custom Floodlight variables use the keys `U1=`, `U2=`, and so on, and can take any values that you choose to pass to them. You can use them to track virtually any type of data that you collect about your customers, such as the genre of movie that a customer purchases, the country to which the item is shipped, and so on. Custom Floodlight variables may not be used to pass any data that could be used or recognized as personally identifiable information (PII). Example: `custom_variables { fields { "U1": value { number_value: 123.4 }, "U2": value { string_value: "MyVariable2" }, "U3": value { string_value: "MyVariable3" } } }` Acceptable values for keys are "U1" through "U100", inclusive. String values must be less than 64 characters long, and cannot contain the following characters: `"<>`. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the Floodlight group. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the Floodlight group. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `web_tag_type` | String | Required. The web tag type enabled for the Floodlight group. |
| `active_view_config` | String | The Active View video viewability metric configuration for the Floodlight group. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |
| `lookback_window` | String | Required. The lookback window for the Floodlight group. Both click_days and impression_days are required. Acceptable values for both are `0` to `90`, inclusive. |
| `custom_variables` | HashMap<String, String> | User-defined custom variables owned by the Floodlight group. Use custom Floodlight variables to create reporting data that is tailored to your unique business needs. Custom Floodlight variables use the keys `U1=`, `U2=`, and so on, and can take any values that you choose to pass to them. You can use them to track virtually any type of data that you collect about your customers, such as the genre of movie that a customer purchases, the country to which the item is shipped, and so on. Custom Floodlight variables may not be used to pass any data that could be used or recognized as personally identifiable information (PII). Example: `custom_variables { fields { "U1": value { number_value: 123.4 }, "U2": value { string_value: "MyVariable2" }, "U3": value { string_value: "MyVariable3" } } }` Acceptable values for keys are "U1" through "U100", inclusive. String values must be less than 64 characters long, and cannot contain the following characters: `"<>`. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the Floodlight group. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the Floodlight group. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access floodlight_group outputs
floodlight_group_id = floodlight_group.id
floodlight_group_web_tag_type = floodlight_group.web_tag_type
floodlight_group_active_view_config = floodlight_group.active_view_config
floodlight_group_floodlight_group_id = floodlight_group.floodlight_group_id
floodlight_group_lookback_window = floodlight_group.lookback_window
floodlight_group_custom_variables = floodlight_group.custom_variables
floodlight_group_display_name = floodlight_group.display_name
floodlight_group_name = floodlight_group.name
```

---


### Operation

Gets the latest state of an asynchronous SDF download task operation. Clients should poll this method at intervals of 30 seconds.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `metadata` | HashMap<String, String> | Service-specific metadata associated with the operation. It typically contains progress information and common metadata such as create time. Some services might not provide such metadata. Any method that returns a long-running operation should document the metadata type, if any. |
| `done` | bool | If the value is `false`, it means the operation is still in progress. If `true`, the operation is completed, and either `error` or `response` is available. |
| `error` | String | The error result of the operation in case of failure or cancellation. |
| `name` | String | The server-assigned name, which is only unique within the same service that originally returns it. If you use the default HTTP mapping, the `name` should be a resource name ending with `operations/{unique_id}`. |
| `response` | HashMap<String, String> | The normal, successful response of the operation. If the original method returns no data on success, such as `Delete`, the response is `google.protobuf.Empty`. If the original method is standard `Get`/`Create`/`Update`, the response should be the resource. For other methods, the response should have the type `XxxResponse`, where `Xxx` is the original method name. For example, if the original method name is `TakeSnapshot()`, the inferred response type is `TakeSnapshotResponse`. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access operation outputs
operation_id = operation.id
operation_metadata = operation.metadata
operation_done = operation.done
operation_error = operation.error
operation_name = operation.name
operation_response = operation.response
```

---


### Line_item

Creates a new line item. Returns the newly created line item if successful. YouTube & Partners line items cannot be created or updated using the API.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the line item was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `bid_strategy` | String |  | Required. The bidding strategy of the line item. |
| `conversion_counting` | String |  | The conversion tracking setting of the line item. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not the line item can spend its budget and bid on inventory. * For CreateLineItem method, only `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` is allowed. To activate a line item, use UpdateLineItem method and update the status to `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` after creation. * A line item cannot be changed back to `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` status from any other status. * If the line item's parent insertion order is not active, the line item can't spend its budget even if its own status is `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`. |
| `insertion_order_id` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the insertion order that the line item belongs to. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the line item. |
| `flight` | String |  | Required. The start and end time of the line item's flight. |
| `line_item_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the line item. Assigned by the system. |
| `frequency_cap` | String |  | Required. The impression frequency cap settings of the line item. The max_impressions field in this settings object must be used if assigning a limited cap. |
| `partner_revenue_model` | String |  | Required. The partner revenue model setting of the line item. |
| `partner_costs` | Vec<String> |  | The partner costs associated with the line item. If absent or empty in CreateLineItem method, the newly created line item will inherit partner costs from its parent insertion order. |
| `budget` | String |  | Required. The budget allocation setting of the line item. |
| `creative_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of the creatives associated with the line item. |
| `pacing` | String |  | Required. The budget spending speed setting of the line item. |
| `reservation_type` | String |  | Output only. The reservation type of the line item. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the line item belongs to. |
| `warning_messages` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The warning messages generated by the line item. These warnings do not block saving the line item, but some may block the line item from running. |
| `exclude_new_exchanges` | bool |  | Whether to exclude new exchanges from automatically being targeted by the line item. This field is false by default. |
| `inventory_source_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of the private inventory sources assigned to the line item. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the line item. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `line_item_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of the line item. |
| `integration_details` | String |  | Integration details of the line item. |
| `mobile_app` | String |  | The mobile app promoted by the line item. This is applicable only when line_item_type is either `LINE_ITEM_TYPE_DISPLAY_MOBILE_APP_INSTALL` or `LINE_ITEM_TYPE_VIDEO_MOBILE_APP_INSTALL`. |
| `campaign_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the campaign that the line item belongs to. |
| `targeting_expansion` | String |  | The [optimized targeting](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/12060859) settings of the line item. This config is only applicable for display, video, or audio line items that use automated bidding and positively target eligible audience lists. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the line item belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the line item was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `bid_strategy` | String | Required. The bidding strategy of the line item. |
| `conversion_counting` | String | The conversion tracking setting of the line item. |
| `entity_status` | String | Required. Controls whether or not the line item can spend its budget and bid on inventory. * For CreateLineItem method, only `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` is allowed. To activate a line item, use UpdateLineItem method and update the status to `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` after creation. * A line item cannot be changed back to `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` status from any other status. * If the line item's parent insertion order is not active, the line item can't spend its budget even if its own status is `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`. |
| `insertion_order_id` | String | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the insertion order that the line item belongs to. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the line item. |
| `flight` | String | Required. The start and end time of the line item's flight. |
| `line_item_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the line item. Assigned by the system. |
| `frequency_cap` | String | Required. The impression frequency cap settings of the line item. The max_impressions field in this settings object must be used if assigning a limited cap. |
| `partner_revenue_model` | String | Required. The partner revenue model setting of the line item. |
| `partner_costs` | Vec<String> | The partner costs associated with the line item. If absent or empty in CreateLineItem method, the newly created line item will inherit partner costs from its parent insertion order. |
| `budget` | String | Required. The budget allocation setting of the line item. |
| `creative_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of the creatives associated with the line item. |
| `pacing` | String | Required. The budget spending speed setting of the line item. |
| `reservation_type` | String | Output only. The reservation type of the line item. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the line item belongs to. |
| `warning_messages` | Vec<String> | Output only. The warning messages generated by the line item. These warnings do not block saving the line item, but some may block the line item from running. |
| `exclude_new_exchanges` | bool | Whether to exclude new exchanges from automatically being targeted by the line item. This field is false by default. |
| `inventory_source_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of the private inventory sources assigned to the line item. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the line item. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `line_item_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of the line item. |
| `integration_details` | String | Integration details of the line item. |
| `mobile_app` | String | The mobile app promoted by the line item. This is applicable only when line_item_type is either `LINE_ITEM_TYPE_DISPLAY_MOBILE_APP_INSTALL` or `LINE_ITEM_TYPE_VIDEO_MOBILE_APP_INSTALL`. |
| `campaign_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the campaign that the line item belongs to. |
| `targeting_expansion` | String | The [optimized targeting](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/12060859) settings of the line item. This config is only applicable for display, video, or audio line items that use automated bidding and positively target eligible audience lists. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create line_item
line_item = provider.displayvideo_api.Line_item {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the line item belongs to.
}

# Access line_item outputs
line_item_id = line_item.id
line_item_update_time = line_item.update_time
line_item_bid_strategy = line_item.bid_strategy
line_item_conversion_counting = line_item.conversion_counting
line_item_entity_status = line_item.entity_status
line_item_insertion_order_id = line_item.insertion_order_id
line_item_name = line_item.name
line_item_flight = line_item.flight
line_item_line_item_id = line_item.line_item_id
line_item_frequency_cap = line_item.frequency_cap
line_item_partner_revenue_model = line_item.partner_revenue_model
line_item_partner_costs = line_item.partner_costs
line_item_budget = line_item.budget
line_item_creative_ids = line_item.creative_ids
line_item_pacing = line_item.pacing
line_item_reservation_type = line_item.reservation_type
line_item_advertiser_id = line_item.advertiser_id
line_item_warning_messages = line_item.warning_messages
line_item_exclude_new_exchanges = line_item.exclude_new_exchanges
line_item_inventory_source_ids = line_item.inventory_source_ids
line_item_display_name = line_item.display_name
line_item_line_item_type = line_item.line_item_type
line_item_integration_details = line_item.integration_details
line_item_mobile_app = line_item.mobile_app
line_item_campaign_id = line_item.campaign_id
line_item_targeting_expansion = line_item.targeting_expansion
```

### Inventory_source_group

Creates a new inventory source group. Returns the newly created inventory source group if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the inventory source group. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `inventory_source_group_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source group. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source group. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the inventory source group. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `inventory_source_group_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source group. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source group. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create inventory_source_group
inventory_source_group = provider.displayvideo_api.Inventory_source_group {
}

# Access inventory_source_group outputs
inventory_source_group_id = inventory_source_group.id
inventory_source_group_display_name = inventory_source_group.display_name
inventory_source_group_inventory_source_group_id = inventory_source_group.inventory_source_group_id
inventory_source_group_name = inventory_source_group.name
```

### Campaign

Creates a new campaign. Returns the newly created campaign if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the campaign. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the campaign was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not the insertion orders under this campaign can spend their budgets and bid on inventory. * Accepted values are `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`, `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED`, and `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED`. * For CreateCampaign method, `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` is not allowed. |
| `campaign_budgets` | Vec<String> |  | The list of budgets available to this campaign. If this field is not set, the campaign uses an unlimited budget. |
| `campaign_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the campaign. Assigned by the system. |
| `campaign_goal` | String |  | Required. The goal of the campaign. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the campaign. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the campaign belongs to. |
| `frequency_cap` | String |  | Required. The frequency cap setting of the campaign. |
| `campaign_flight` | String |  | Required. The planned spend and duration of the campaign. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the campaign belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the campaign. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the campaign was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `entity_status` | String | Required. Controls whether or not the insertion orders under this campaign can spend their budgets and bid on inventory. * Accepted values are `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`, `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED`, and `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED`. * For CreateCampaign method, `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` is not allowed. |
| `campaign_budgets` | Vec<String> | The list of budgets available to this campaign. If this field is not set, the campaign uses an unlimited budget. |
| `campaign_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the campaign. Assigned by the system. |
| `campaign_goal` | String | Required. The goal of the campaign. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the campaign. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the campaign belongs to. |
| `frequency_cap` | String | Required. The frequency cap setting of the campaign. |
| `campaign_flight` | String | Required. The planned spend and duration of the campaign. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create campaign
campaign = provider.displayvideo_api.Campaign {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the campaign belongs to.
}

# Access campaign outputs
campaign_id = campaign.id
campaign_name = campaign.name
campaign_update_time = campaign.update_time
campaign_entity_status = campaign.entity_status
campaign_campaign_budgets = campaign.campaign_budgets
campaign_campaign_id = campaign.campaign_id
campaign_campaign_goal = campaign.campaign_goal
campaign_display_name = campaign.display_name
campaign_advertiser_id = campaign.advertiser_id
campaign_frequency_cap = campaign.frequency_cap
campaign_campaign_flight = campaign.campaign_flight
```

### Site

Creates a site in a channel.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the site. |
| `url_or_app_id` | String |  | Required. The app ID or URL of the site. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `channel_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the parent channel in which the site will be created. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | The ID of the advertiser that owns the parent channel. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListSites` method to retrieve the next page of results. |
| `sites` | Vec<String> | The list of sites. This list will be absent if empty. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create site
site = provider.displayvideo_api.Site {
    channel_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the parent channel in which the site will be created.
    advertiser_id = "value"  # The ID of the advertiser that owns the parent channel.
}

# Access site outputs
site_id = site.id
site_next_page_token = site.next_page_token
site_sites = site.sites
```

---


### Creative

Creates a new creative. Returns the newly created creative if successful. A ["Standard" user role](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/2723011) or greater for the parent advertiser or partner is required to make this request.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `hosting_source` | String |  | Required. Indicates where the creative is hosted. |
| `expand_on_hover` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates the creative will automatically expand on hover. Optional and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `ias_campaign_monitoring` | bool |  | Indicates whether Integral Ad Science (IAS) campaign monitoring is enabled. To enable this for the creative, make sure the Advertiser.creative_config.ias_client_id has been set to your IAS client ID. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the creative was created. Assigned by the system. |
| `vpaid` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires VPAID (Digital Video Player-Ad Interface). Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `universal_ad_id` | String |  | Optional. An optional creative identifier provided by a registry that is unique across all platforms. Universal Ad ID is part of the VAST 4.0 standard. It can be modified after the creative is created. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `creative_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of the creative. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not the creative can serve. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` * `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the creative. |
| `counter_events` | Vec<String> |  | Counter events for a rich media creative. Counters track the number of times that a user interacts with any part of a rich media creative in a specified way (mouse-overs, mouse-outs, clicks, taps, data loading, keyboard entries, etc.). Any event that can be captured in the creative can be recorded as a counter. Leave it empty or unset for creatives containing image assets only. |
| `skip_offset` | String |  | Amount of time to play the video before the skip button appears. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `require_ping_for_attribution` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates that the creative will wait for a return ping for attribution. Only valid when using a Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad with a third-party ad server parameter and the ${DC_DBM_TOKEN} macro. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives or third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `oba_icon` | String |  | Specifies the OBA icon for a video creative. This field is only supported in following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `timer_events` | Vec<String> |  | Timer custom events for a rich media creative. Timers track the time during which a user views and interacts with a specified part of a rich media creative. A creative can have multiple timer events, each timed independently. Leave it empty or unset for creatives containing image assets only. |
| `assets` | Vec<String> |  | Required. Assets associated to this creative. |
| `appended_tag` | String |  | Third-party HTML tracking tag to be appended to the creative tag. |
| `expanding_direction` | String |  | Optional. Specifies the expanding direction of the creative. Required and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `integration_code` | String |  | ID information used to link this creative to an external system. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a length of no more than 10,000 characters. |
| `transcodes` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. Audio/Video transcodes. Display & Video 360 transcodes the main asset into a number of alternative versions that use different file formats or have different properties (resolution, audio bit rate, and video bit rate), each designed for specific video players or bandwidths. These transcodes give a publisher's system more options to choose from for each impression on your video and ensures that the appropriate file serves based on the viewer’s connection and screen size. This field is only supported in following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `companion_creative_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of companion creatives for a video creative. You can assign existing display creatives (with image or HTML5 assets) to serve surrounding the publisher's video player. Companions display around the video player while the video is playing and remain after the video has completed. Creatives contain additional dimensions can not be companion creatives. This field is only supported for following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the creative. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `html5_video` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires HTML5 Video support. Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `mp3_audio` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports MP3. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the creative was last updated, either by the user or system (e.g. creative review). Assigned by the system. |
| `creative_attributes` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. A list of attributes of the creative that is generated by the system. |
| `creative_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the creative. Assigned by the system. |
| `additional_dimensions` | Vec<String> |  | Additional dimensions. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_LIGHTBOX` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` If this field is specified, width_pixels and height_pixels are both required and must be greater than or equal to 0. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to. |
| `notes` | String |  | User notes for this creative. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a length of no more than 20,000 characters. |
| `cm_placement_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the Campaign Manager 360 placement associated with the creative. This field is only applicable for creatives that are synced from Campaign Manager. |
| `js_tracker_url` | String |  | JavaScript measurement URL from supported third-party verification providers (ComScore, DoubleVerify, IAS, Moat). HTML script tags are not supported. This field is only writeable in following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `ogg_audio` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports OGG. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `require_mraid` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates that the creative requires MRAID (Mobile Rich Media Ad Interface Definitions system). Set this if the creative relies on mobile gestures for interactivity, such as swiping or tapping. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `media_duration` | String |  | Output only. Media duration of the creative. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` |
| `exit_events` | Vec<String> |  | Required. Exit events for this creative. An exit (also known as a click tag) is any area in your creative that someone can click or tap to open an advertiser's landing page. Every creative must include at least one exit. You can add an exit to your creative in any of the following ways: * Use Google Web Designer's tap area. * Define a JavaScript variable called "clickTag". * Use the Enabler (Enabler.exit()) to track exits in rich media formats. |
| `cm_tracking_ad` | String |  | The Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad associated with the creative. Optional for the following creative_type when created by an advertiser that uses both Campaign Manager 360 and third-party ad serving: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` Output only for other cases. |
| `dimensions` | String |  | Required. Primary dimensions of the creative. Applicable to all creative types. The value of width_pixels and height_pixels defaults to `0` when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `dynamic` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates whether the creative is dynamic. |
| `review_status` | String |  | Output only. The current status of the creative review process. |
| `require_html5` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates that the creative relies on HTML5 to render properly. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `tracker_urls` | Vec<String> |  | Tracking URLs for analytics providers or third-party ad technology vendors. The URLs must start with https (except on inventory that doesn't require SSL compliance). If using macros in your URL, use only macros supported by Display & Video 360. Standard URLs only, no IMG or SCRIPT tags. This field is only writeable in following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `skippable` | bool |  | Whether the user can choose to skip a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `vast_tag_url` | String |  | Optional. The URL of the VAST tag for a third-party VAST tag creative. Required and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `third_party_urls` | Vec<String> |  | Tracking URLs from third parties to track interactions with a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `progress_offset` | String |  | Amount of time to play the video before counting a view. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `line_item_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The IDs of the line items this creative is associated with. To associate a creative to a line item, use LineItem.creative_ids instead. |
| `third_party_tag` | String |  | Optional. The original third-party tag used for the creative. Required and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `hosting_source` | String | Required. Indicates where the creative is hosted. |
| `expand_on_hover` | bool | Optional. Indicates the creative will automatically expand on hover. Optional and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |

| `vpaid` | bool | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires VPAID (Digital Video Player-Ad Interface). Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. It can be modified after the creative is created. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `creative_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of the creative. |

| `oba_icon` | String | Specifies the OBA icon for a video creative. This field is only supported in following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |

| `ogg_audio` | bool | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports OGG. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `require_mraid` | bool | Optional. Indicates that the creative requires MRAID (Mobile Rich Media Ad Interface Definitions system). Set this if the creative relies on mobile gestures for interactivity, such as swiping or tapping. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `media_duration` | String | Output only. Media duration of the creative. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` |
| `exit_events` | Vec<String> | Required. Exit events for this creative. An exit (also known as a click tag) is any area in your creative that someone can click or tap to open an advertiser's landing page. Every creative must include at least one exit. You can add an exit to your creative in any of the following ways: * Use Google Web Designer's tap area. * Define a JavaScript variable called "clickTag". * Use the Enabler (Enabler.exit()) to track exits in rich media formats. |
| `cm_tracking_ad` | String | The Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad associated with the creative. Optional for the following creative_type when created by an advertiser that uses both Campaign Manager 360 and third-party ad serving: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` Output only for other cases. |
| `dimensions` | String | Required. Primary dimensions of the creative. Applicable to all creative types. The value of width_pixels and height_pixels defaults to `0` when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `dynamic` | bool | Output only. Indicates whether the creative is dynamic. |
| `review_status` | String | Output only. The current status of the creative review process. |
| `require_html5` | bool | Optional. Indicates that the creative relies on HTML5 to render properly. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `tracker_urls` | Vec<String> | Tracking URLs for analytics providers or third-party ad technology vendors. The URLs must start with https (except on inventory that doesn't require SSL compliance). If using macros in your URL, use only macros supported by Display & Video 360. Standard URLs only, no IMG or SCRIPT tags. This field is only writeable in following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `skippable` | bool | Whether the user can choose to skip a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `vast_tag_url` | String | Optional. The URL of the VAST tag for a third-party VAST tag creative. Required and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `third_party_urls` | Vec<String> | Tracking URLs from third parties to track interactions with a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `progress_offset` | String | Amount of time to play the video before counting a view. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `line_item_ids` | Vec<String> | Output only. The IDs of the line items this creative is associated with. To associate a creative to a line item, use LineItem.creative_ids instead. |
| `third_party_tag` | String | Optional. The original third-party tag used for the creative. Required and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create creative
creative = provider.displayvideo_api.Creative {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to.
}

# Access creative outputs
creative_id = creative.id
creative_hosting_source = creative.hosting_source
creative_expand_on_hover = creative.expand_on_hover
creative_ias_campaign_monitoring = creative.ias_campaign_monitoring
creative_create_time = creative.create_time
creative_vpaid = creative.vpaid
creative_universal_ad_id = creative.universal_ad_id
creative_creative_type = creative.creative_type
creative_entity_status = creative.entity_status
creative_name = creative.name
creative_counter_events = creative.counter_events
creative_skip_offset = creative.skip_offset
creative_require_ping_for_attribution = creative.require_ping_for_attribution
creative_oba_icon = creative.oba_icon
creative_timer_events = creative.timer_events
creative_assets = creative.assets
creative_appended_tag = creative.appended_tag
creative_expanding_direction = creative.expanding_direction
creative_integration_code = creative.integration_code
creative_transcodes = creative.transcodes
creative_companion_creative_ids = creative.companion_creative_ids
creative_display_name = creative.display_name
creative_html5_video = creative.html5_video
creative_mp3_audio = creative.mp3_audio
creative_update_time = creative.update_time
creative_creative_attributes = creative.creative_attributes
creative_creative_id = creative.creative_id
creative_additional_dimensions = creative.additional_dimensions
creative_advertiser_id = creative.advertiser_id
creative_notes = creative.notes
creative_cm_placement_id = creative.cm_placement_id
creative_js_tracker_url = creative.js_tracker_url
creative_ogg_audio = creative.ogg_audio
creative_require_mraid = creative.require_mraid
creative_media_duration = creative.media_duration
creative_exit_events = creative.exit_events
creative_cm_tracking_ad = creative.cm_tracking_ad
creative_dimensions = creative.dimensions
creative_dynamic = creative.dynamic
creative_review_status = creative.review_status
creative_require_html5 = creative.require_html5
creative_tracker_urls = creative.tracker_urls
creative_skippable = creative.skippable
creative_vast_tag_url = creative.vast_tag_url
creative_third_party_urls = creative.third_party_urls
creative_progress_offset = creative.progress_offset
creative_line_item_ids = creative.line_item_ids
creative_third_party_tag = creative.third_party_tag
```

### Channel

Creates a new channel. Returns the newly created channel if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `channel_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the channel. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the channel. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | The ID of the advertiser that owns the channel. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the channel. |
| `negatively_targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel negatively. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | The ID of the partner that owns the channel. |
| `positively_targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel positively. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | The ID of the advertiser that owns the created channel. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `channel_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the channel. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the channel. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | The ID of the advertiser that owns the channel. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the channel. |
| `negatively_targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel negatively. |
| `partner_id` | String | The ID of the partner that owns the channel. |
| `positively_targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel positively. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create channel
channel = provider.displayvideo_api.Channel {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # The ID of the advertiser that owns the created channel.
}

# Access channel outputs
channel_id = channel.id
channel_channel_id = channel.channel_id
channel_display_name = channel.display_name
channel_advertiser_id = channel.advertiser_id
channel_name = channel.name
channel_negatively_targeted_line_item_count = channel.negatively_targeted_line_item_count
channel_partner_id = channel.partner_id
channel_positively_targeted_line_item_count = channel.positively_targeted_line_item_count
```

### Media

Uploads media. Upload is supported on the URI `/upload/media/{resource_name=**}?upload_type=media.` **Note**: Upload requests will not be successful without including `upload_type=media` query string.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `resource_name` | String |  | Name of the media resource. |
| `resource_name` | String | ✅ | Name of the media that is being downloaded. See ReadRequest.resource_name. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `resource_name` | String | Name of the media resource. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create media
media = provider.displayvideo_api.Media {
    resource_name = "value"  # Name of the media that is being downloaded. See ReadRequest.resource_name.
}

# Access media outputs
media_id = media.id
media_resource_name = media.resource_name
```

### Manual_trigger

Creates a new manual trigger. Returns the newly created manual trigger if successful. **Warning:** Line Items using manual triggers no longer serve in Display & Video 360. This method will sunset on August 1, 2023. Read our [feature deprecation announcement](/display-video/api/deprecations#features.manual_triggers) for more information.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the manual trigger. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `state` | String |  | Output only. The state of the manual trigger. Will be set to the `INACTIVE` state upon creation. |
| `latest_activation_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp of the trigger's latest activation. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that the manual trigger belongs to. |
| `activation_duration_minutes` | String |  | Required. The maximum duration of each activation in minutes. Must be between 1 and 360 inclusive. After this duration, the trigger will be automatically deactivated. |
| `trigger_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the manual trigger. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the manual trigger. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that the manual trigger belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the manual trigger. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `state` | String | Output only. The state of the manual trigger. Will be set to the `INACTIVE` state upon creation. |
| `latest_activation_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp of the trigger's latest activation. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that the manual trigger belongs to. |
| `activation_duration_minutes` | String | Required. The maximum duration of each activation in minutes. Must be between 1 and 360 inclusive. After this duration, the trigger will be automatically deactivated. |
| `trigger_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the manual trigger. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the manual trigger. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create manual_trigger
manual_trigger = provider.displayvideo_api.Manual_trigger {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that the manual trigger belongs to.
}

# Access manual_trigger outputs
manual_trigger_id = manual_trigger.id
manual_trigger_display_name = manual_trigger.display_name
manual_trigger_state = manual_trigger.state
manual_trigger_latest_activation_time = manual_trigger.latest_activation_time
manual_trigger_advertiser_id = manual_trigger.advertiser_id
manual_trigger_activation_duration_minutes = manual_trigger.activation_duration_minutes
manual_trigger_trigger_id = manual_trigger.trigger_id
manual_trigger_name = manual_trigger.name
```

### User

Creates a new user. Returns the newly created user if successful. This method has unique authentication requirements. Read the prerequisites in our [Managing Users guide](/display-video/api/guides/users/overview#prerequisites) before using this method. The "Try this method" feature does not work for this method.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `assigned_user_roles` | Vec<String> |  | The assigned user roles. Required in CreateUser. Output only in UpdateUser. Can only be updated through BulkEditAssignedUserRoles. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the user. |
| `email` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The email address used to identify the user. |
| `user_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the user. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the user. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `last_login_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the user last logged in DV360 UI. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `assigned_user_roles` | Vec<String> | The assigned user roles. Required in CreateUser. Output only in UpdateUser. Can only be updated through BulkEditAssignedUserRoles. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the user. |
| `email` | String | Required. Immutable. The email address used to identify the user. |
| `user_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the user. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the user. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `last_login_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the user last logged in DV360 UI. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create user
user = provider.displayvideo_api.User {
}

# Access user outputs
user_id = user.id
user_assigned_user_roles = user.assigned_user_roles
user_name = user.name
user_email = user.email
user_user_id = user.user_id
user_display_name = user.display_name
user_last_login_time = user.last_login_time
```

### Negative_keyword

Creates a negative keyword in a negative keyword list.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the negative keyword. |
| `keyword_value` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The negatively targeted keyword, for example `car insurance`. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. Maximum number of characters is 80. Maximum number of words is 10. Valid characters are restricted to ASCII characters only. The only URL-escaping permitted is for representing whitespace between words. Leading or trailing whitespace is ignored. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the parent negative keyword list belongs. |
| `negative_keyword_list_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the parent negative keyword list in which the negative keyword will be created. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListNegativeKeywords` method to retrieve the next page of results. |
| `negative_keywords` | Vec<String> | The list of negative keywords. This list will be absent if empty. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create negative_keyword
negative_keyword = provider.displayvideo_api.Negative_keyword {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the parent negative keyword list belongs.
    negative_keyword_list_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the parent negative keyword list in which the negative keyword will be created.
}

# Access negative_keyword outputs
negative_keyword_id = negative_keyword.id
negative_keyword_next_page_token = negative_keyword.next_page_token
negative_keyword_negative_keywords = negative_keyword.negative_keywords
```

---


### Guaranteed_order

Creates a new guaranteed order. Returns the newly created guaranteed order if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `status` | String |  | The status settings of the guaranteed order. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `default_campaign_id` | String |  | The ID of the default campaign that is assigned to the guaranteed order. The default campaign must belong to the default advertiser. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the guaranteed order. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of advertisers with read access to the guaranteed order. This field must not include the advertiser assigned to read_write_advertiser_id if it is set. All advertisers in this field must belong to read_write_partner_id or the same partner as read_write_advertiser_id. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the guaranteed order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `publisher_name` | String |  | Required. The publisher name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `legacy_guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The legacy ID of the guaranteed order. Assigned by the original exchange. The legacy ID is unique within one exchange, but is not guaranteed to be unique across all guaranteed orders. This ID is used in SDF and UI. |
| `default_advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The ID of default advertiser of the guaranteed order. The default advertiser is either the read_write_advertiser_id or, if that is not set, the first advertiser listed in read_advertiser_ids. Otherwise, there is no default advertiser. |
| `exchange` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The exchange where the guaranteed order originated. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique identifier of the guaranteed order. The guaranteed order IDs have the format `{exchange}-{legacy_guaranteed_order_id}`. |
| `read_access_inherited` | bool |  | Whether all advertisers of read_write_partner_id have read access to the guaranteed order. Only applicable if read_write_partner_id is set. If True, overrides read_advertiser_ids. |
| `read_write_advertiser_id` | String |  | The advertiser with read/write access to the guaranteed order. This is also the default advertiser of the guaranteed order. |
| `read_write_partner_id` | String |  | The partner with read/write access to the guaranteed order. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `status` | String | The status settings of the guaranteed order. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `default_campaign_id` | String | The ID of the default campaign that is assigned to the guaranteed order. The default campaign must belong to the default advertiser. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the guaranteed order. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of advertisers with read access to the guaranteed order. This field must not include the advertiser assigned to read_write_advertiser_id if it is set. All advertisers in this field must belong to read_write_partner_id or the same partner as read_write_advertiser_id. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the guaranteed order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `publisher_name` | String | Required. The publisher name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `legacy_guaranteed_order_id` | String | Output only. The legacy ID of the guaranteed order. Assigned by the original exchange. The legacy ID is unique within one exchange, but is not guaranteed to be unique across all guaranteed orders. This ID is used in SDF and UI. |
| `default_advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The ID of default advertiser of the guaranteed order. The default advertiser is either the read_write_advertiser_id or, if that is not set, the first advertiser listed in read_advertiser_ids. Otherwise, there is no default advertiser. |
| `exchange` | String | Required. Immutable. The exchange where the guaranteed order originated. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String | Output only. The unique identifier of the guaranteed order. The guaranteed order IDs have the format `{exchange}-{legacy_guaranteed_order_id}`. |
| `read_access_inherited` | bool | Whether all advertisers of read_write_partner_id have read access to the guaranteed order. Only applicable if read_write_partner_id is set. If True, overrides read_advertiser_ids. |
| `read_write_advertiser_id` | String | The advertiser with read/write access to the guaranteed order. This is also the default advertiser of the guaranteed order. |
| `read_write_partner_id` | String | The partner with read/write access to the guaranteed order. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create guaranteed_order
guaranteed_order = provider.displayvideo_api.Guaranteed_order {
}

# Access guaranteed_order outputs
guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.id
guaranteed_order_status = guaranteed_order.status
guaranteed_order_display_name = guaranteed_order.display_name
guaranteed_order_default_campaign_id = guaranteed_order.default_campaign_id
guaranteed_order_name = guaranteed_order.name
guaranteed_order_read_advertiser_ids = guaranteed_order.read_advertiser_ids
guaranteed_order_update_time = guaranteed_order.update_time
guaranteed_order_publisher_name = guaranteed_order.publisher_name
guaranteed_order_legacy_guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.legacy_guaranteed_order_id
guaranteed_order_default_advertiser_id = guaranteed_order.default_advertiser_id
guaranteed_order_exchange = guaranteed_order.exchange
guaranteed_order_guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.guaranteed_order_id
guaranteed_order_read_access_inherited = guaranteed_order.read_access_inherited
guaranteed_order_read_write_advertiser_id = guaranteed_order.read_write_advertiser_id
guaranteed_order_read_write_partner_id = guaranteed_order.read_write_partner_id
```

---


### Asset

Uploads an asset. Returns the ID of the newly uploaded asset if successful. The asset file size should be no more than 10 MB for images, 200 MB for ZIP files, and 1 GB for videos. Must be used within the [multipart media upload process](/display-video/api/guides/how-tos/upload#multipart). Examples using provided client libraries can be found in our [Creating Creatives guide](/display-video/api/guides/creating-creatives/overview#upload_an_asset).

**Operations**: ✅ Create

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `filename` | String |  | Required. The filename of the asset, including the file extension. The filename must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the advertiser this asset belongs to. |



#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create asset
asset = provider.displayvideo_api.Asset {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the advertiser this asset belongs to.
}

```

---


### Inventory_source

Creates a new inventory source. Returns the newly created inventory source if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `inventory_source_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source. Assigned by the system. |
| `time_range` | String |  | The time range when this inventory source starts and stops serving. |
| `status` | String |  | The status settings of the inventory source. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the inventory source was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `read_partner_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The IDs of partners with read-only access to the inventory source. All advertisers of partners in this field inherit read-only access to the inventory source. |
| `publisher_name` | String |  | The publisher/seller name of the inventory source. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Immutable. The ID of the guaranteed order that this inventory source belongs to. Only applicable when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`. |
| `creative_configs` | Vec<String> |  | The creative requirements of the inventory source. Not applicable for auction packages. |
| `exchange` | String |  | The exchange to which the inventory source belongs. |
| `display_name` | String |  | The display name of the inventory source. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `inventory_source_product_type` | String |  | Output only. The product type of the inventory source, denoting the way through which it sells inventory. |
| `read_write_accessors` | String |  | The partner or advertisers that have read/write access to the inventory source. Output only when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`, in which case the read/write accessors are inherited from the parent guaranteed order. Required when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED`. If commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED` and a partner is set in this field, all advertisers under this partner will automatically have read-only access to the inventory source. These advertisers will not be included in read_advertiser_ids. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The IDs of advertisers with read-only access to the inventory source. |
| `deal_id` | String |  | The ID in the exchange space that uniquely identifies the inventory source. Must be unique across buyers within each exchange but not necessarily unique across exchanges. |
| `rate_details` | String |  | Required. The rate details of the inventory source. |
| `delivery_method` | String |  | The delivery method of the inventory source. * For non-guaranteed inventory sources, the only acceptable value is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. * For guaranteed inventory sources, acceptable values are `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_TAG` and `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. |
| `inventory_source_type` | String |  | Denotes the type of the inventory source. |
| `commitment` | String |  | Whether the inventory source has a guaranteed or non-guaranteed delivery. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `inventory_source_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source. Assigned by the system. |
| `time_range` | String | The time range when this inventory source starts and stops serving. |
| `status` | String | The status settings of the inventory source. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the inventory source was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `read_partner_ids` | Vec<String> | Output only. The IDs of partners with read-only access to the inventory source. All advertisers of partners in this field inherit read-only access to the inventory source. |
| `publisher_name` | String | The publisher/seller name of the inventory source. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String | Immutable. The ID of the guaranteed order that this inventory source belongs to. Only applicable when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`. |
| `creative_configs` | Vec<String> | The creative requirements of the inventory source. Not applicable for auction packages. |
| `exchange` | String | The exchange to which the inventory source belongs. |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the inventory source. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `inventory_source_product_type` | String | Output only. The product type of the inventory source, denoting the way through which it sells inventory. |
| `read_write_accessors` | String | The partner or advertisers that have read/write access to the inventory source. Output only when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`, in which case the read/write accessors are inherited from the parent guaranteed order. Required when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED`. If commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED` and a partner is set in this field, all advertisers under this partner will automatically have read-only access to the inventory source. These advertisers will not be included in read_advertiser_ids. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | Output only. The IDs of advertisers with read-only access to the inventory source. |
| `deal_id` | String | The ID in the exchange space that uniquely identifies the inventory source. Must be unique across buyers within each exchange but not necessarily unique across exchanges. |
| `rate_details` | String | Required. The rate details of the inventory source. |
| `delivery_method` | String | The delivery method of the inventory source. * For non-guaranteed inventory sources, the only acceptable value is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. * For guaranteed inventory sources, acceptable values are `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_TAG` and `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. |
| `inventory_source_type` | String | Denotes the type of the inventory source. |
| `commitment` | String | Whether the inventory source has a guaranteed or non-guaranteed delivery. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create inventory_source
inventory_source = provider.displayvideo_api.Inventory_source {
}

# Access inventory_source outputs
inventory_source_id = inventory_source.id
inventory_source_inventory_source_id = inventory_source.inventory_source_id
inventory_source_time_range = inventory_source.time_range
inventory_source_status = inventory_source.status
inventory_source_update_time = inventory_source.update_time
inventory_source_read_partner_ids = inventory_source.read_partner_ids
inventory_source_publisher_name = inventory_source.publisher_name
inventory_source_guaranteed_order_id = inventory_source.guaranteed_order_id
inventory_source_creative_configs = inventory_source.creative_configs
inventory_source_exchange = inventory_source.exchange
inventory_source_display_name = inventory_source.display_name
inventory_source_inventory_source_product_type = inventory_source.inventory_source_product_type
inventory_source_read_write_accessors = inventory_source.read_write_accessors
inventory_source_name = inventory_source.name
inventory_source_read_advertiser_ids = inventory_source.read_advertiser_ids
inventory_source_deal_id = inventory_source.deal_id
inventory_source_rate_details = inventory_source.rate_details
inventory_source_delivery_method = inventory_source.delivery_method
inventory_source_inventory_source_type = inventory_source.inventory_source_type
inventory_source_commitment = inventory_source.commitment
```
