### Assigned_targeting_option

Assigns a targeting option to a line item. Returns the assigned targeting option if successful. Requests to this endpoint cannot be made concurrently with the following requests updating the same line item: * lineItems.bulkEditAssignedTargetingOptions * lineItems.bulkUpdate * lineItems.patch * DeleteLineItemAssignedTargetingOption YouTube & Partners line items cannot be created or updated using the API.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `viewability_details` | String |  | Viewability details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY`. You can only target one viewability option per resource. |
| `keyword_details` | String |  | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_KEYWORD`. A maximum of 5000 direct negative keywords can be assigned to a resource. No limit on number of positive keywords that can be assigned. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name for this assigned targeting option. |
| `content_duration_details` | String |  | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_DURATION`. |
| `inheritance` | String |  | Output only. The inheritance status of the assigned targeting option. |
| `inventory_source_details` | String |  | Inventory source details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE`. |
| `on_screen_position_details` | String |  | On screen position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ON_SCREEN_POSITION`. |
| `poi_details` | String |  | POI details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_POI`. |
| `channel_details` | String |  | Channel details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL`. |
| `sensitive_category_exclusion_details` | String |  | Sensitive category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION`. Sensitive categories are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level sensitive category exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude sensitive categories in addition to advertiser exclusions, but can't override them. |
| `url_details` | String |  | URL details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_URL`. |
| `app_category_details` | String |  | App category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_APP_CATEGORY`. |
| `carrier_and_isp_details` | String |  | Carrier and ISP details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CARRIER_AND_ISP`. |
| `audience_group_details` | String |  | Audience targeting details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIENCE_GROUP`. You can only target one audience group option per resource. |
| `device_type_details` | String |  | Device Type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE`. |
| `digital_content_label_exclusion_details` | String |  | Digital content label details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION`. Digital content labels are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level digital content label exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude content labels in addition to advertiser exclusions, but can't override them. A line item won't serve if all the digital content labels are excluded. |
| `gender_details` | String |  | Gender details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER`. |
| `inventory_source_group_details` | String |  | Inventory source group details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE_GROUP`. |
| `omid_details` | String |  | Open Measurement enabled inventory details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_OMID`. |
| `regional_location_list_details` | String |  | Regional location list details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_REGIONAL_LOCATION_LIST`. |
| `assigned_targeting_option_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned targeting option. The ID is only unique within a given resource and targeting type. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `targeting_type` | String |  | Output only. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. |
| `content_outstream_position_details` | String |  | Content outstream position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION`. |
| `third_party_verifier_details` | String |  | Third party verification details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_THIRD_PARTY_VERIFIER`. |
| `browser_details` | String |  | Browser details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BROWSER`. |
| `business_chain_details` | String |  | Business chain details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`. |
| `app_details` | String |  | App details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_APP`. |
| `exchange_details` | String |  | Exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE`. |
| `user_rewarded_content_details` | String |  | User rewarded content details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_USER_REWARDED_CONTENT`. |
| `category_details` | String |  | Category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CATEGORY`. Targeting a category will also target its subcategories. If a category is excluded from targeting and a subcategory is included, the exclusion will take precedence. |
| `operating_system_details` | String |  | Operating system details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_OPERATING_SYSTEM`. |
| `proximity_location_list_details` | String |  | Proximity location list details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_PROXIMITY_LOCATION_LIST`. |
| `content_genre_details` | String |  | Content genre details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_GENRE`. |
| `language_details` | String |  | Language details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_LANGUAGE`. |
| `parental_status_details` | String |  | Parental status details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS`. |
| `content_instream_position_details` | String |  | Content instream position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION`. |
| `authorized_seller_status_details` | String |  | Authorized seller status details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUTHORIZED_SELLER_STATUS`. You can only target one authorized seller status option per resource. If a resource doesn't have an authorized seller status option, all authorized sellers indicated as DIRECT or RESELLER in the ads.txt file are targeted by default. |
| `geo_region_details` | String |  | Geographic region details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION`. |
| `native_content_position_details` | String |  | Native content position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION`. |
| `age_range_details` | String |  | Age range details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE`. |
| `video_player_size_details` | String |  | Video player size details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE`. |
| `day_and_time_details` | String |  | Day and time details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DAY_AND_TIME`. |
| `audio_content_type_details` | String |  | Audio content type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIO_CONTENT_TYPE`. |
| `negative_keyword_list_details` | String |  | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NEGATIVE_KEYWORD_LIST`. A maximum of 4 negative keyword lists can be assigned to a resource. |
| `sub_exchange_details` | String |  | Sub-exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SUB_EXCHANGE`. |
| `content_stream_type_details` | String |  | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the TargetingType is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_STREAM_TYPE`. |
| `device_make_model_details` | String |  | Device make and model details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_MAKE_MODEL`. |
| `household_income_details` | String |  | Household income details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME`. |
| `environment_details` | String |  | Environment details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT`. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the advertiser the line item belongs to. |
| `line_item_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the line item the assigned targeting option will belong to. |
| `targeting_type` | String | ✅ | Required. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. Supported targeting types include: * `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_APP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_APP_CATEGORY` * `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIENCE_GROUP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIO_CONTENT_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_AUTHORIZED_SELLER_STATUS` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BROWSER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CARRIER_AND_ISP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CATEGORY` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_DURATION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_GENRE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_STREAM_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DAY_AND_TIME` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_MAKE_MODEL` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT` * `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME` * `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE_GROUP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_KEYWORD` * `TARGETING_TYPE_LANGUAGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_NEGATIVE_KEYWORD_LIST` * `TARGETING_TYPE_OMID` * `TARGETING_TYPE_ON_SCREEN_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_OPERATING_SYSTEM` * `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS` * `TARGETING_TYPE_POI` * `TARGETING_TYPE_PROXIMITY_LOCATION_LIST` * `TARGETING_TYPE_REGIONAL_LOCATION_LIST` * `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_SUB_EXCHANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_THIRD_PARTY_VERIFIER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_URL` * `TARGETING_TYPE_USER_REWARDED_CONTENT` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY` |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `viewability_details` | String | Viewability details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY`. You can only target one viewability option per resource. |

| `native_content_position_details` | String | Native content position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION`. |
| `age_range_details` | String | Age range details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE`. |
| `video_player_size_details` | String | Video player size details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE`. |
| `day_and_time_details` | String | Day and time details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DAY_AND_TIME`. |
| `audio_content_type_details` | String | Audio content type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIO_CONTENT_TYPE`. |
| `negative_keyword_list_details` | String | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NEGATIVE_KEYWORD_LIST`. A maximum of 4 negative keyword lists can be assigned to a resource. |
| `sub_exchange_details` | String | Sub-exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SUB_EXCHANGE`. |
| `content_stream_type_details` | String | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the TargetingType is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_STREAM_TYPE`. |
| `device_make_model_details` | String | Device make and model details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_MAKE_MODEL`. |
| `household_income_details` | String | Household income details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME`. |
| `environment_details` | String | Environment details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT`. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create assigned_targeting_option
assigned_targeting_option = provider.displayvideo_api.Assigned_targeting_option {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the advertiser the line item belongs to.
    line_item_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the line item the assigned targeting option will belong to.
    targeting_type = "value"  # Required. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. Supported targeting types include: * `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_APP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_APP_CATEGORY` * `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIENCE_GROUP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIO_CONTENT_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_AUTHORIZED_SELLER_STATUS` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BROWSER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CARRIER_AND_ISP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CATEGORY` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_DURATION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_GENRE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_STREAM_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DAY_AND_TIME` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_MAKE_MODEL` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT` * `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME` * `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE_GROUP` * `TARGETING_TYPE_KEYWORD` * `TARGETING_TYPE_LANGUAGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_NEGATIVE_KEYWORD_LIST` * `TARGETING_TYPE_OMID` * `TARGETING_TYPE_ON_SCREEN_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_OPERATING_SYSTEM` * `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS` * `TARGETING_TYPE_POI` * `TARGETING_TYPE_PROXIMITY_LOCATION_LIST` * `TARGETING_TYPE_REGIONAL_LOCATION_LIST` * `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_SUB_EXCHANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_THIRD_PARTY_VERIFIER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_URL` * `TARGETING_TYPE_USER_REWARDED_CONTENT` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY`
}

# Access assigned_targeting_option outputs
```

### Custom_bidding_algorithm

Creates a new custom bidding algorithm. Returns the newly created custom bidding algorithm if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_state` | String |  | Output only. The status of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `model_readiness` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The state of custom bidding model readiness for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the state of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `advertiser_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_state` | String | Output only. The status of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `entity_status` | String | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `partner_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `model_readiness` | Vec<String> | Output only. The state of custom bidding model readiness for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the state of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create custom_bidding_algorithm
custom_bidding_algorithm = provider.displayvideo_api.Custom_bidding_algorithm {
}

# Access custom_bidding_algorithm outputs
custom_bidding_algorithm_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.id
custom_bidding_algorithm_advertiser_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.advertiser_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_state = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_state
custom_bidding_algorithm_name = custom_bidding_algorithm.name
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_type = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_type
custom_bidding_algorithm_shared_advertiser_ids = custom_bidding_algorithm.shared_advertiser_ids
custom_bidding_algorithm_entity_status = custom_bidding_algorithm.entity_status
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_display_name = custom_bidding_algorithm.display_name
custom_bidding_algorithm_partner_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.partner_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_model_readiness = custom_bidding_algorithm.model_readiness
```

### Script

Creates a new custom bidding script. Returns the newly created script if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `state` | String |  | Output only. The state of the custom bidding script. |
| `custom_bidding_script_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding script. |
| `script` | String |  | The reference to the uploaded script file. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The time when the script was created. |
| `active` | bool |  | Output only. Whether the script is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `errors` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. Error details of a rejected custom bidding script. This field will only be populated when state is REJECTED. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding script. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm the script belongs to. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the script. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `state` | String | Output only. The state of the custom bidding script. |
| `custom_bidding_script_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding script. |
| `script` | String | The reference to the uploaded script file. |
| `create_time` | String | Output only. The time when the script was created. |
| `active` | bool | Output only. Whether the script is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `errors` | Vec<String> | Output only. Error details of a rejected custom bidding script. This field will only be populated when state is REJECTED. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding script. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm the script belongs to. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create script
script = provider.displayvideo_api.Script {
    custom_bidding_algorithm_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the script.
}

# Access script outputs
script_id = script.id
script_state = script.state
script_custom_bidding_script_id = script.custom_bidding_script_id
script_script = script.script
script_create_time = script.create_time
script_active = script.active
script_errors = script.errors
script_name = script.name
script_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = script.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
```

### Assigned_inventory_source

Creates an assignment between an inventory source and an inventory source group.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the assigned inventory source. |
| `assigned_inventory_source_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned inventory source. The ID is only unique within a given inventory source group. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `inventory_source_id` | String |  | Required. The ID of the inventory source entity being targeted. |
| `inventory_source_group_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the inventory source group to which the assignment will be assigned. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListAssignedInventorySources` method to retrieve the next page of results. |
| `assigned_inventory_sources` | Vec<String> | The list of assigned inventory sources. This list will be absent if empty. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create assigned_inventory_source
assigned_inventory_source = provider.displayvideo_api.Assigned_inventory_source {
    inventory_source_group_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the inventory source group to which the assignment will be assigned.
}

# Access assigned_inventory_source outputs
assigned_inventory_source_id = assigned_inventory_source.id
assigned_inventory_source_next_page_token = assigned_inventory_source.next_page_token
assigned_inventory_source_assigned_inventory_sources = assigned_inventory_source.assigned_inventory_sources
```

### Partner

Bulk edits targeting options under a single partner. The operation will delete the assigned targeting options provided in BulkEditPartnerAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest.deleteRequests and then create the assigned targeting options provided in BulkEditPartnerAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest.createRequests .

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `delete_requests` | Vec<String> |  | The assigned targeting options to delete in batch, specified as a list of `DeleteAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest`. Supported targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` |
| `create_requests` | Vec<String> |  | The assigned targeting options to create in batch, specified as a list of `CreateAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest`. Supported targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the partner. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `general_config` | String | General settings of the partner. |
| `ad_server_config` | String | Ad server related settings of the partner. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the partner was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the partner. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `entity_status` | String | Output only. The status of the partner. |
| `data_access_config` | String | Settings that control how partner data may be accessed. |
| `exchange_config` | String | Settings that control which exchanges are enabled for the partner. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the partner. |
| `partner_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the partner. Assigned by the system. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create partner
partner = provider.displayvideo_api.Partner {
    partner_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the partner.
}

# Access partner outputs
partner_id = partner.id
partner_general_config = partner.general_config
partner_ad_server_config = partner.ad_server_config
partner_update_time = partner.update_time
partner_display_name = partner.display_name
partner_entity_status = partner.entity_status
partner_data_access_config = partner.data_access_config
partner_exchange_config = partner.exchange_config
partner_name = partner.name
partner_partner_id = partner.partner_id
```

### First_and_third_party_audience

Creates a FirstAndThirdPartyAudience. Only supported for the following audience_type: * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID`

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `mobile_device_id_list` | String |  | Input only. A list of mobile device IDs to define the initial audience members. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `description` | String |  | The user-provided description of the audience. Only applicable to first party audiences. |
| `audience_source` | String |  | Output only. The source of the audience. |
| `active_display_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for the Display network in the past month. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only returned in GET request. |
| `display_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for the Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only returned in GET request. |
| `youtube_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for YouTube network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `gmail_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for Gmail network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `app_id` | String |  | The app_id matches with the type of the mobile_device_ids being uploaded. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `display_mobile_web_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated mobile web audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `audience_type` | String |  | The type of the audience. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the first and third party audience. |
| `contact_info_list` | String |  | Input only. A list of contact information to define the initial audience members. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` |
| `display_name` | String |  | The display name of the first and third party audience. |
| `first_and_third_party_audience_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the first and third party audience. Assigned by the system. |
| `membership_duration_days` | String |  | The duration in days that an entry remains in the audience after the qualifying event. If the audience has no expiration, set the value of this field to 10000. Otherwise, the set value must be greater than 0 and less than or equal to 540. Only applicable to first party audiences. This field is required if one of the following audience_type is used: * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `display_mobile_app_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated mobile app audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `display_desktop_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated desktop audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `first_and_third_party_audience_type` | String |  | Whether the audience is a first or third party audience. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `mobile_device_id_list` | String | Input only. A list of mobile device IDs to define the initial audience members. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `description` | String | The user-provided description of the audience. Only applicable to first party audiences. |
| `audience_source` | String | Output only. The source of the audience. |
| `active_display_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated audience size for the Display network in the past month. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only returned in GET request. |
| `display_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated audience size for the Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only returned in GET request. |
| `youtube_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated audience size for YouTube network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `gmail_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated audience size for Gmail network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `app_id` | String | The app_id matches with the type of the mobile_device_ids being uploaded. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `display_mobile_web_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated mobile web audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `audience_type` | String | The type of the audience. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the first and third party audience. |
| `contact_info_list` | String | Input only. A list of contact information to define the initial audience members. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the first and third party audience. |
| `first_and_third_party_audience_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the first and third party audience. Assigned by the system. |
| `membership_duration_days` | String | The duration in days that an entry remains in the audience after the qualifying event. If the audience has no expiration, set the value of this field to 10000. Otherwise, the set value must be greater than 0 and less than or equal to 540. Only applicable to first party audiences. This field is required if one of the following audience_type is used: * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `display_mobile_app_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated mobile app audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `display_desktop_audience_size` | String | Output only. The estimated desktop audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `first_and_third_party_audience_type` | String | Whether the audience is a first or third party audience. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create first_and_third_party_audience
first_and_third_party_audience = provider.displayvideo_api.First_and_third_party_audience {
}

# Access first_and_third_party_audience outputs
first_and_third_party_audience_id = first_and_third_party_audience.id
first_and_third_party_audience_mobile_device_id_list = first_and_third_party_audience.mobile_device_id_list
first_and_third_party_audience_description = first_and_third_party_audience.description
first_and_third_party_audience_audience_source = first_and_third_party_audience.audience_source
first_and_third_party_audience_active_display_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.active_display_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_display_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.display_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_youtube_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.youtube_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_gmail_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.gmail_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_app_id = first_and_third_party_audience.app_id
first_and_third_party_audience_display_mobile_web_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.display_mobile_web_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_audience_type = first_and_third_party_audience.audience_type
first_and_third_party_audience_name = first_and_third_party_audience.name
first_and_third_party_audience_contact_info_list = first_and_third_party_audience.contact_info_list
first_and_third_party_audience_display_name = first_and_third_party_audience.display_name
first_and_third_party_audience_first_and_third_party_audience_id = first_and_third_party_audience.first_and_third_party_audience_id
first_and_third_party_audience_membership_duration_days = first_and_third_party_audience.membership_duration_days
first_and_third_party_audience_display_mobile_app_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.display_mobile_app_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_display_desktop_audience_size = first_and_third_party_audience.display_desktop_audience_size
first_and_third_party_audience_first_and_third_party_audience_type = first_and_third_party_audience.first_and_third_party_audience_type
```

### Assigned_location

Creates an assignment between a location and a location list.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the assigned location. |
| `targeting_option_id` | String |  | Required. The ID of the targeting option assigned to the location list. |
| `assigned_location_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned location. The ID is only unique within a location list. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `location_list_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the location list for which the assignment will be created. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the location list belongs. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListAssignedLocations` method to retrieve the next page of results. |
| `assigned_locations` | Vec<String> | The list of assigned locations. This list will be absent if empty. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create assigned_location
assigned_location = provider.displayvideo_api.Assigned_location {
    location_list_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the location list for which the assignment will be created.
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the location list belongs.
}

# Access assigned_location outputs
assigned_location_id = assigned_location.id
assigned_location_next_page_token = assigned_location.next_page_token
assigned_location_assigned_locations = assigned_location.assigned_locations
```

### Insertion_order

Creates a new insertion order. Returns the newly created insertion order if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `reservation_type` | String |  | Output only. The reservation type of the insertion order. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the insertion order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `billable_outcome` | String |  | Immutable. The billable outcome of the insertion order. Outcome based buying is deprecated. `BILLABLE_OUTCOME_PAY_PER_IMPRESSION` is the only valid value. |
| `budget` | String |  | Required. The budget allocation settings of the insertion order. |
| `campaign_id` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the campaign that the insertion order belongs to. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the insertion order. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not the insertion order can spend its budget and bid on inventory. * For CreateInsertionOrder method, only `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` is allowed. To activate an insertion order, use UpdateInsertionOrder method and update the status to `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` after creation. * An insertion order cannot be changed back to `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` status from any other status. * An insertion order cannot be set to `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` if its parent campaign is not active. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the insertion order belongs to. |
| `insertion_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the insertion order. Assigned by the system. |
| `performance_goal` | String |  | Required. Performance goal of the insertion order. |
| `bid_strategy` | String |  | The bidding strategy of the insertion order. By default, fixed_bid is set. |
| `frequency_cap` | String |  | Required. The frequency capping setting of the insertion order. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the insertion order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `insertion_order_type` | String |  | The type of insertion order. If this field is unspecified in creation, the value defaults to `RTB`. |
| `integration_details` | String |  | Additional integration details of the insertion order. |
| `pacing` | String |  | Required. The budget spending speed setting of the insertion order. |
| `partner_costs` | Vec<String> |  | The partner costs associated with the insertion order. If absent or empty in CreateInsertionOrder method, the newly created insertion order will inherit partner costs from the partner settings. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the insertion order belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `reservation_type` | String | Output only. The reservation type of the insertion order. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the insertion order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `billable_outcome` | String | Immutable. The billable outcome of the insertion order. Outcome based buying is deprecated. `BILLABLE_OUTCOME_PAY_PER_IMPRESSION` is the only valid value. |
| `budget` | String | Required. The budget allocation settings of the insertion order. |
| `campaign_id` | String | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the campaign that the insertion order belongs to. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the insertion order. |
| `entity_status` | String | Required. Controls whether or not the insertion order can spend its budget and bid on inventory. * For CreateInsertionOrder method, only `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` is allowed. To activate an insertion order, use UpdateInsertionOrder method and update the status to `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` after creation. * An insertion order cannot be changed back to `ENTITY_STATUS_DRAFT` status from any other status. * An insertion order cannot be set to `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` if its parent campaign is not active. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the insertion order belongs to. |
| `insertion_order_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the insertion order. Assigned by the system. |
| `performance_goal` | String | Required. Performance goal of the insertion order. |
| `bid_strategy` | String | The bidding strategy of the insertion order. By default, fixed_bid is set. |
| `frequency_cap` | String | Required. The frequency capping setting of the insertion order. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the insertion order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `insertion_order_type` | String | The type of insertion order. If this field is unspecified in creation, the value defaults to `RTB`. |
| `integration_details` | String | Additional integration details of the insertion order. |
| `pacing` | String | Required. The budget spending speed setting of the insertion order. |
| `partner_costs` | Vec<String> | The partner costs associated with the insertion order. If absent or empty in CreateInsertionOrder method, the newly created insertion order will inherit partner costs from the partner settings. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create insertion_order
insertion_order = provider.displayvideo_api.Insertion_order {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the insertion order belongs to.
}

# Access insertion_order outputs
insertion_order_id = insertion_order.id
insertion_order_reservation_type = insertion_order.reservation_type
insertion_order_update_time = insertion_order.update_time
insertion_order_billable_outcome = insertion_order.billable_outcome
insertion_order_budget = insertion_order.budget
insertion_order_campaign_id = insertion_order.campaign_id
insertion_order_name = insertion_order.name
insertion_order_entity_status = insertion_order.entity_status
insertion_order_advertiser_id = insertion_order.advertiser_id
insertion_order_insertion_order_id = insertion_order.insertion_order_id
insertion_order_performance_goal = insertion_order.performance_goal
insertion_order_bid_strategy = insertion_order.bid_strategy
insertion_order_frequency_cap = insertion_order.frequency_cap
insertion_order_display_name = insertion_order.display_name
insertion_order_insertion_order_type = insertion_order.insertion_order_type
insertion_order_integration_details = insertion_order.integration_details
insertion_order_pacing = insertion_order.pacing
insertion_order_partner_costs = insertion_order.partner_costs
```

### Targeting_option

Searches for targeting options of a given type based on the given search terms.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Required. The Advertiser this request is being made in the context of. |
| `business_chain_search_terms` | String |  | Search terms for Business Chain targeting options. Can only be used when targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`. |
| `geo_region_search_terms` | String |  | Search terms for geo region targeting options. Can only be used when targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION`. |
| `page_token` | String |  | A token identifying a page of results the server should return. Typically, this is the value of next_page_token returned from the previous call to `SearchTargetingOptions` method. If not specified, the first page of results will be returned. |
| `poi_search_terms` | String |  | Search terms for POI targeting options. Can only be used when targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_POI`. |
| `page_size` | i64 |  | Requested page size. Must be between `1` and `200`. If unspecified will default to `100`. Returns error code `INVALID_ARGUMENT` if an invalid value is specified. |
| `targeting_type` | String | ✅ | Required. The type of targeting options to retrieve. Accepted values are: * `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_POI` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN` |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `device_type_details` | String | Device type details. |
| `business_chain_details` | String | Business chain resource details. |
| `omid_details` | String | Open Measurement enabled inventory details. |
| `operating_system_details` | String | Operating system resources details. |
| `content_genre_details` | String | Content genre resource details. |
| `on_screen_position_details` | String | On screen position details. |
| `geo_region_details` | String | Geographic region resource details. |
| `targeting_type` | String | Output only. The type of this targeting option. |
| `audio_content_type_details` | String | Audio content type details. |
| `app_category_details` | String | App category details. |
| `age_range_details` | String | Age range details. |
| `carrier_and_isp_details` | String | Carrier and ISP details. |
| `content_stream_type_details` | String | Content stream type resource details. |
| `sub_exchange_details` | String | Sub-exchange details. |
| `browser_details` | String | Browser details. |
| `targeting_option_id` | String | Output only. A unique identifier for this targeting option. The tuple {`targeting_type`, `targeting_option_id`} will be unique. |
| `language_details` | String | Language resource details. |
| `sensitive_category_details` | String | Sensitive Category details. |
| `video_player_size_details` | String | Video player size details. |
| `exchange_details` | String | Exchange details. |
| `user_rewarded_content_details` | String | User rewarded content details. |
| `environment_details` | String | Environment details. |
| `digital_content_label_details` | String | Digital content label details. |
| `content_duration_details` | String | Content duration resource details. |
| `content_instream_position_details` | String | Content instream position details. |
| `viewability_details` | String | Viewability resource details. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name for this targeting option. |
| `device_make_model_details` | String | Device make and model resource details. |
| `household_income_details` | String | Household income details. |
| `authorized_seller_status_details` | String | Authorized seller status resource details. |
| `poi_details` | String | POI resource details. |
| `content_outstream_position_details` | String | Content outstream position details. |
| `gender_details` | String | Gender details. |
| `native_content_position_details` | String | Native content position details. |
| `category_details` | String | Category resource details. |
| `parental_status_details` | String | Parental status details. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl

    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create targeting_option

    targeting_type = "value"  # Required. The type of targeting options to retrieve. Accepted values are: * `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_POI` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`
}

# Access targeting_option outputs
targeting_option_id = targeting_option.id
targeting_option_device_type_details = targeting_option.device_type_details

targeting_option_operating_system_details = targeting_option.operating_system_details

targeting_option_on_screen_position_details = targeting_option.on_screen_position_details
targeting_option_geo_region_details = targeting_option.geo_region_details
targeting_option_targeting_type = targeting_option.targeting_type
targeting_option_audio_content_type_details = targeting_option.audio_content_type_details
targeting_option_app_category_details = targeting_option.app_category_details
targeting_option_age_range_details = targeting_option.age_range_details
targeting_option_carrier_and_isp_details = targeting_option.carrier_and_isp_details
targeting_option_content_stream_type_details = targeting_option.content_stream_type_details
targeting_option_sub_exchange_details = targeting_option.sub_exchange_details
targeting_option_browser_details = targeting_option.browser_details
targeting_option_targeting_option_id = targeting_option.targeting_option_id
targeting_option_language_details = targeting_option.language_details
targeting_option_sensitive_category_details = targeting_option.sensitive_category_details
targeting_option_video_player_size_details = targeting_option.video_player_size_details
targeting_option_exchange_details = targeting_option.exchange_details
targeting_option_user_rewarded_content_details = targeting_option.user_rewarded_content_details
targeting_option_environment_details = targeting_option.environment_details
targeting_option_digital_content_label_details = targeting_option.digital_content_label_details
targeting_option_content_duration_details = targeting_option.content_duration_details
```

| `targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this negative keyword list. |
| `negative_keyword_list_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the negative keyword list. Assigned by the system. |

### Invoice

Lists invoices posted for an advertiser in a given month. Invoices generated by billing profiles with a "Partner" invoice level are not retrievable through this method.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `invoices` | Vec<String> | The list of invoices. This list will be absent if empty. |
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListInvoices` method to retrieve the next page of results. This token will be absent if there are no more invoices to return. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access invoice outputs
invoice_id = invoice.id
invoice_invoices = invoice.invoices
invoice_next_page_token = invoice.next_page_token
```

### Sdfdownloadtask

Creates an SDF Download Task. Returns an Operation. An SDF Download Task is a long-running, asynchronous operation. The metadata type of this operation is SdfDownloadTaskMetadata. If the request is successful, the response type of the operation is SdfDownloadTask. The response will not include the download files, which must be retrieved with media.download. The state of operation can be retrieved with sdfdownloadtask.operations.get. Any errors can be found in the error.message. Note that error.details is expected to be empty.

**Operations**: ✅ Create

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `partner_id` | String |  | The ID of the partner to download SDF for. |
| `version` | String |  | Required. The SDF version of the downloaded file. If set to `SDF_VERSION_UNSPECIFIED`, this will default to the version specified by the advertiser or partner identified by `root_id`. An advertiser inherits its SDF version from its partner unless configured otherwise. |
| `id_filter` | String |  | Filters on entities by their entity IDs. |
| `inventory_source_filter` | String |  | Filters on Inventory Sources by their IDs. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | The ID of the advertiser to download SDF for. |
| `parent_entity_filter` | String |  | Filters on selected file types. The entities in each file are filtered by a chosen set of filter entities. The filter entities must be the same type as, or a parent type of, the selected file types. |



#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create sdfdownloadtask
sdfdownloadtask = provider.displayvideo_api.Sdfdownloadtask {
}

```

---


### Media

Downloads media. Download is supported on the URI `/download/{resource_name=**}?alt=media.` **Note**: Download requests will not be successful without including `alt=media` query string.

|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

```kcl
    project = "my-project-id"
}

```

### Operation

Gets the latest state of an asynchronous SDF download task operation. Clients should poll this method at intervals of 30 seconds.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `metadata` | HashMap<String, String> | Service-specific metadata associated with the operation. It typically contains progress information and common metadata such as create time. Some services might not provide such metadata. Any method that returns a long-running operation should document the metadata type, if any. |
| `response` | HashMap<String, String> | The normal response of the operation in case of success. If the original method returns no data on success, such as `Delete`, the response is `google.protobuf.Empty`. If the original method is standard `Get`/`Create`/`Update`, the response should be the resource. For other methods, the response should have the type `XxxResponse`, where `Xxx` is the original method name. For example, if the original method name is `TakeSnapshot()`, the inferred response type is `TakeSnapshotResponse`. |
| `done` | bool | If the value is `false`, it means the operation is still in progress. If `true`, the operation is completed, and either `error` or `response` is available. |
| `error` | String | The error result of the operation in case of failure or cancellation. |
| `name` | String | The server-assigned name, which is only unique within the same service that originally returns it. If you use the default HTTP mapping, the `name` should be a resource name ending with `operations/{unique_id}`. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access operation outputs
operation_id = operation.id
operation_metadata = operation.metadata
operation_response = operation.response
operation_done = operation.done
operation_error = operation.error
operation_name = operation.name
```

### Guaranteed_order

Creates a new guaranteed order. Returns the newly created guaranteed order if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `status` | String |  | The status settings of the guaranteed order. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the guaranteed order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `exchange` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The exchange where the guaranteed order originated. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the guaranteed order. |
| `publisher_name` | String |  | Required. The publisher name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `read_access_inherited` | bool |  | Whether all advertisers of read_write_partner_id have read access to the guaranteed order. Only applicable if read_write_partner_id is set. If True, overrides read_advertiser_ids. |
| `default_advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The ID of default advertiser of the guaranteed order. The default advertiser is either the read_write_advertiser_id or, if that is not set, the first advertiser listed in read_advertiser_ids. Otherwise, there is no default advertiser. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique identifier of the guaranteed order. The guaranteed order IDs have the format `{exchange}-{legacy_guaranteed_order_id}`. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of advertisers with read access to the guaranteed order. This field must not include the advertiser assigned to read_write_advertiser_id if it is set. All advertisers in this field must belong to read_write_partner_id or the same partner as read_write_advertiser_id. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `default_campaign_id` | String |  | The ID of the default campaign that is assigned to the guaranteed order. The default campaign must belong to the default advertiser. |
| `read_write_advertiser_id` | String |  | The advertiser with read/write access to the guaranteed order. This is also the default advertiser of the guaranteed order. |
| `legacy_guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The legacy ID of the guaranteed order. Assigned by the original exchange. The legacy ID is unique within one exchange, but is not guaranteed to be unique across all guaranteed orders. This ID is used in SDF and UI. |
| `read_write_partner_id` | String |  | The partner with read/write access to the guaranteed order. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `status` | String | The status settings of the guaranteed order. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the guaranteed order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `exchange` | String | Required. Immutable. The exchange where the guaranteed order originated. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the guaranteed order. |
| `publisher_name` | String | Required. The publisher name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `read_access_inherited` | bool | Whether all advertisers of read_write_partner_id have read access to the guaranteed order. Only applicable if read_write_partner_id is set. If True, overrides read_advertiser_ids. |
| `default_advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The ID of default advertiser of the guaranteed order. The default advertiser is either the read_write_advertiser_id or, if that is not set, the first advertiser listed in read_advertiser_ids. Otherwise, there is no default advertiser. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String | Output only. The unique identifier of the guaranteed order. The guaranteed order IDs have the format `{exchange}-{legacy_guaranteed_order_id}`. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of advertisers with read access to the guaranteed order. This field must not include the advertiser assigned to read_write_advertiser_id if it is set. All advertisers in this field must belong to read_write_partner_id or the same partner as read_write_advertiser_id. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `default_campaign_id` | String | The ID of the default campaign that is assigned to the guaranteed order. The default campaign must belong to the default advertiser. |
| `read_write_advertiser_id` | String | The advertiser with read/write access to the guaranteed order. This is also the default advertiser of the guaranteed order. |
| `legacy_guaranteed_order_id` | String | Output only. The legacy ID of the guaranteed order. Assigned by the original exchange. The legacy ID is unique within one exchange, but is not guaranteed to be unique across all guaranteed orders. This ID is used in SDF and UI. |
| `read_write_partner_id` | String | The partner with read/write access to the guaranteed order. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create guaranteed_order
guaranteed_order = provider.displayvideo_api.Guaranteed_order {
}

# Access guaranteed_order outputs
guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.id
guaranteed_order_status = guaranteed_order.status
guaranteed_order_update_time = guaranteed_order.update_time
guaranteed_order_exchange = guaranteed_order.exchange
guaranteed_order_name = guaranteed_order.name
guaranteed_order_publisher_name = guaranteed_order.publisher_name
guaranteed_order_read_access_inherited = guaranteed_order.read_access_inherited
guaranteed_order_default_advertiser_id = guaranteed_order.default_advertiser_id
guaranteed_order_guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.guaranteed_order_id
guaranteed_order_read_advertiser_ids = guaranteed_order.read_advertiser_ids
guaranteed_order_display_name = guaranteed_order.display_name
guaranteed_order_default_campaign_id = guaranteed_order.default_campaign_id
guaranteed_order_read_write_advertiser_id = guaranteed_order.read_write_advertiser_id
guaranteed_order_legacy_guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.legacy_guaranteed_order_id
guaranteed_order_read_write_partner_id = guaranteed_order.read_write_partner_id
```

### Custom_bidding_algorithm

Creates a new custom bidding algorithm. Returns the newly created custom bidding algorithm if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `model_details` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The details of custom bidding models for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the details of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `model_details` | Vec<String> | Output only. The details of custom bidding models for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the details of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `partner_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `entity_status` | String | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create custom_bidding_algorithm

}

# Access custom_bidding_algorithm outputs

custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_type = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_type
```

### Inventory_source

Creates a new inventory source. Returns the newly created inventory source if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String |  | The display name of the inventory source. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `deal_id` | String |  | The ID in the exchange space that uniquely identifies the inventory source. Must be unique across buyers within each exchange but not necessarily unique across exchanges. |
| `delivery_method` | String |  | The delivery method of the inventory source. * For non-guaranteed inventory sources, the only acceptable value is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. * For guaranteed inventory sources, acceptable values are `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_TAG` and `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. |
| `publisher_name` | String |  | The publisher/seller name of the inventory source. |
| `creative_configs` | Vec<String> |  | The creative requirements of the inventory source. Not applicable for auction packages. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source. |
| `rate_details` | String |  | Required. The rate details of the inventory source. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Immutable. The ID of the guaranteed order that this inventory source belongs to. Only applicable when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`. |
| `inventory_source_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source. Assigned by the system. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the inventory source was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `read_write_accessors` | String |  | The partner or advertisers that have read/write access to the inventory source. Output only when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`, in which case the read/write accessors are inherited from the parent guaranteed order. Required when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED`. If commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED` and a partner is set in this field, all advertisers under this partner will automatically have read-only access to the inventory source. These advertisers will not be included in read_advertiser_ids. |
| `time_range` | String |  | The time range when this inventory source starts and stops serving. |
| `inventory_source_type` | String |  | Denotes the type of the inventory source. |
| `read_partner_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The IDs of partners with read-only access to the inventory source. All advertisers of partners in this field inherit read-only access to the inventory source. |
| `commitment` | String |  | Whether the inventory source has a guaranteed or non-guaranteed delivery. |
| `status` | String |  | The status settings of the inventory source. |
| `inventory_source_product_type` | String |  | Output only. The product type of the inventory source, denoting the way through which it sells inventory. |
| `exchange` | String |  | The exchange to which the inventory source belongs. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The IDs of advertisers with read-only access to the inventory source. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the inventory source. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `deal_id` | String | The ID in the exchange space that uniquely identifies the inventory source. Must be unique across buyers within each exchange but not necessarily unique across exchanges. |
| `delivery_method` | String | The delivery method of the inventory source. * For non-guaranteed inventory sources, the only acceptable value is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. * For guaranteed inventory sources, acceptable values are `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_TAG` and `INVENTORY_SOURCE_DELIVERY_METHOD_PROGRAMMATIC`. |
| `publisher_name` | String | The publisher/seller name of the inventory source. |
| `creative_configs` | Vec<String> | The creative requirements of the inventory source. Not applicable for auction packages. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source. |
| `rate_details` | String | Required. The rate details of the inventory source. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String | Immutable. The ID of the guaranteed order that this inventory source belongs to. Only applicable when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`. |
| `inventory_source_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source. Assigned by the system. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the inventory source was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `read_write_accessors` | String | The partner or advertisers that have read/write access to the inventory source. Output only when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_GUARANTEED`, in which case the read/write accessors are inherited from the parent guaranteed order. Required when commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED`. If commitment is `INVENTORY_SOURCE_COMMITMENT_NON_GUARANTEED` and a partner is set in this field, all advertisers under this partner will automatically have read-only access to the inventory source. These advertisers will not be included in read_advertiser_ids. |
| `time_range` | String | The time range when this inventory source starts and stops serving. |
| `inventory_source_type` | String | Denotes the type of the inventory source. |
| `read_partner_ids` | Vec<String> | Output only. The IDs of partners with read-only access to the inventory source. All advertisers of partners in this field inherit read-only access to the inventory source. |
| `commitment` | String | Whether the inventory source has a guaranteed or non-guaranteed delivery. |
| `status` | String | The status settings of the inventory source. |
| `inventory_source_product_type` | String | Output only. The product type of the inventory source, denoting the way through which it sells inventory. |
| `exchange` | String | The exchange to which the inventory source belongs. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | Output only. The IDs of advertisers with read-only access to the inventory source. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider

    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create inventory_source

}

# Access inventory_source outputs

inventory_source_display_name = inventory_source.display_name
inventory_source_deal_id = inventory_source.deal_id
inventory_source_delivery_method = inventory_source.delivery_method
inventory_source_publisher_name = inventory_source.publisher_name
inventory_source_creative_configs = inventory_source.creative_configs
inventory_source_name = inventory_source.name
inventory_source_rate_details = inventory_source.rate_details
inventory_source_guaranteed_order_id = inventory_source.guaranteed_order_id
inventory_source_inventory_source_id = inventory_source.inventory_source_id
inventory_source_update_time = inventory_source.update_time
inventory_source_read_write_accessors = inventory_source.read_write_accessors
inventory_source_time_range = inventory_source.time_range
```
