### Rule

Creates a new rules resource. Returns the newly created rules resource if successful. Requests creating a custom bidding rules resource under an algorithm assigned to a line item will return an error.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `rules` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The reference to the uploaded AlgorithmRules file. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm that the rules resource belongs to. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the rules resource. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the rules resource. |
| `state` | String |  | Output only. The state of the rules resource. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The time when the rules resource was created. |
| `error` | String |  | Output only. Error code of the rejected rules resource. This field will only be populated when the state is `REJECTED`. |
| `active` | bool |  | Output only. Whether the rules resource is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the rules resource. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `rules` | String | Required. Immutable. The reference to the uploaded AlgorithmRules file. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm that the rules resource belongs to. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the rules resource. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the rules resource. |
| `state` | String | Output only. The state of the rules resource. |
| `create_time` | String | Output only. The time when the rules resource was created. |
| `error` | String | Output only. Error code of the rejected rules resource. This field will only be populated when the state is `REJECTED`. |
| `active` | bool | Output only. Whether the rules resource is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create rule
rule = provider.displayvideo_api.Rule {
    custom_bidding_algorithm_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the rules resource.
}

# Access rule outputs
rule_id = rule.id
rule_rules = rule.rules
rule_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = rule.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
rule_name = rule.name
rule_custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id = rule.custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id
rule_state = rule.state
rule_create_time = rule.create_time
rule_error = rule.error
rule_active = rule.active
```

### Assigned_location

Creates an assignment between a location and a location list.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `assigned_location_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned location. The ID is only unique within a location list. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `targeting_option_id` | String |  | Required. The ID of the targeting option assigned to the location list. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the assigned location. |
| `location_list_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the location list for which the assignment will be created. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the location list belongs. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListAssignedLocations` method to retrieve the next page of results. |
| `assigned_locations` | Vec<String> | The list of assigned locations. This list will be absent if empty. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
    project = "my-project-id"
}

    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the location list belongs.
}

# Access assigned_location outputs

assigned_location_next_page_token = assigned_location.next_page_token

```

### Floodlight_group

Gets a Floodlight group.

**Operations**: ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `active_view_config` | String |  | The Active View video viewability metric configuration for the Floodlight group. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |
| `web_tag_type` | String |  | Required. The web tag type enabled for the Floodlight group. |
| `lookback_window` | String |  | Required. The lookback window for the Floodlight group. Both click_days and impression_days are required. Acceptable values for both are `0` to `90`, inclusive. |
| `custom_variables` | HashMap<String, String> |  | User-defined custom variables owned by the Floodlight group. Use custom Floodlight variables to create reporting data that is tailored to your unique business needs. Custom Floodlight variables use the keys `U1=`, `U2=`, and so on, and can take any values that you choose to pass to them. You can use them to track virtually any type of data that you collect about your customers, such as the genre of movie that a customer purchases, the country to which the item is shipped, and so on. Custom Floodlight variables may not be used to pass any data that could be used or recognized as personally identifiable information (PII). Example: `custom_variables { fields { "U1": value { number_value: 123.4 }, "U2": value { string_value: "MyVariable2" }, "U3": value { string_value: "MyVariable3" } } }` Acceptable values for keys are "U1" through "U100", inclusive. String values must be less than 64 characters long, and cannot contain the following characters: `"<>`. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the Floodlight group. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the Floodlight group. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `active_view_config` | String | The Active View video viewability metric configuration for the Floodlight group. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |
| `web_tag_type` | String | Required. The web tag type enabled for the Floodlight group. |
| `lookback_window` | String | Required. The lookback window for the Floodlight group. Both click_days and impression_days are required. Acceptable values for both are `0` to `90`, inclusive. |
| `custom_variables` | HashMap<String, String> | User-defined custom variables owned by the Floodlight group. Use custom Floodlight variables to create reporting data that is tailored to your unique business needs. Custom Floodlight variables use the keys `U1=`, `U2=`, and so on, and can take any values that you choose to pass to them. You can use them to track virtually any type of data that you collect about your customers, such as the genre of movie that a customer purchases, the country to which the item is shipped, and so on. Custom Floodlight variables may not be used to pass any data that could be used or recognized as personally identifiable information (PII). Example: `custom_variables { fields { "U1": value { number_value: 123.4 }, "U2": value { string_value: "MyVariable2" }, "U3": value { string_value: "MyVariable3" } } }` Acceptable values for keys are "U1" through "U100", inclusive. String values must be less than 64 characters long, and cannot contain the following characters: `"<>`. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the Floodlight group. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the Floodlight group. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access floodlight_group outputs
floodlight_group_id = floodlight_group.id
floodlight_group_active_view_config = floodlight_group.active_view_config
floodlight_group_floodlight_group_id = floodlight_group.floodlight_group_id
floodlight_group_web_tag_type = floodlight_group.web_tag_type
floodlight_group_lookback_window = floodlight_group.lookback_window
floodlight_group_custom_variables = floodlight_group.custom_variables
floodlight_group_display_name = floodlight_group.display_name
floodlight_group_name = floodlight_group.name
```

### Partner

Edits targeting options under a single partner. The operation will delete the assigned targeting options provided in BulkEditPartnerAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest.deleteRequests and then create the assigned targeting options provided in BulkEditPartnerAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest.createRequests .

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `create_requests` | Vec<String> |  | The assigned targeting options to create in batch, specified as a list of `CreateAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest`. Supported targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` |
| `delete_requests` | Vec<String> |  | The assigned targeting options to delete in batch, specified as a list of `DeleteAssignedTargetingOptionsRequest`. Supported targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the partner. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `exchange_config` | String | Settings that control which exchanges are enabled for the partner. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the partner was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `data_access_config` | String | Settings that control how partner data may be accessed. |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the partner. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `entity_status` | String | Output only. The status of the partner. |
| `general_config` | String | General settings of the partner. |
| `billing_config` | String | Billing related settings of the partner. |
| `ad_server_config` | String | Ad server related settings of the partner. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the partner. |
| `partner_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the partner. Assigned by the system. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create partner
partner = provider.displayvideo_api.Partner {
    partner_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the partner.
}

# Access partner outputs
partner_id = partner.id
partner_exchange_config = partner.exchange_config
partner_update_time = partner.update_time
partner_data_access_config = partner.data_access_config
partner_display_name = partner.display_name
partner_entity_status = partner.entity_status
partner_general_config = partner.general_config
partner_billing_config = partner.billing_config
partner_ad_server_config = partner.ad_server_config
partner_name = partner.name
partner_partner_id = partner.partner_id
```

### Custom_bidding_algorithm

Creates a new custom bidding algorithm. Returns the newly created custom bidding algorithm if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `entity_status` | String |  | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `third_party_optimization_partner` | String |  | Optional. Immutable. Designates the third party optimization partner that manages this algorithm. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `model_details` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The details of custom bidding models for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the details of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `entity_status` | String | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `third_party_optimization_partner` | String | Optional. Immutable. Designates the third party optimization partner that manages this algorithm. |
| `partner_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `model_details` | Vec<String> | Output only. The details of custom bidding models for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the details of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create custom_bidding_algorithm
custom_bidding_algorithm = provider.displayvideo_api.Custom_bidding_algorithm {
}

# Access custom_bidding_algorithm outputs
custom_bidding_algorithm_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.id
custom_bidding_algorithm_entity_status = custom_bidding_algorithm.entity_status
custom_bidding_algorithm_shared_advertiser_ids = custom_bidding_algorithm.shared_advertiser_ids
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_type = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_type
custom_bidding_algorithm_third_party_optimization_partner = custom_bidding_algorithm.third_party_optimization_partner
custom_bidding_algorithm_partner_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.partner_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_model_details = custom_bidding_algorithm.model_details
custom_bidding_algorithm_name = custom_bidding_algorithm.name
custom_bidding_algorithm_display_name = custom_bidding_algorithm.display_name
custom_bidding_algorithm_advertiser_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.advertiser_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
```

### Media

Uploads media. Upload is supported on the URI `/upload/media/{resource_name=**}?upload_type=media.` **Note**: Upload requests will not be successful without including `upload_type=media` query string.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `resource_name` | String |  | Name of the media resource. |
| `resource_name` | String | ✅ | Name of the media that is being downloaded. See ReadRequest.resource_name. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `resource_name` | String | Name of the media resource. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create media
media = provider.displayvideo_api.Media {
    resource_name = "value"  # Name of the media that is being downloaded. See ReadRequest.resource_name.
}

# Access media outputs
media_id = media.id
media_resource_name = media.resource_name
```

### Advertiser

Creates a new advertiser. Returns the newly created advertiser if successful. **This method regularly experiences high latency.** We recommend [increasing your default timeout](/display-video/api/guides/best-practices/timeouts#client_library_timeout) to avoid errors.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `data_access_config` | String |  | Settings that control how advertiser data may be accessed. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the advertiser was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `serving_config` | String |  | Targeting settings related to ad serving of the advertiser. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser. Assigned by the system. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that the advertiser belongs to. |
| `billing_config` | String |  | Required. Billing related settings of the advertiser. |
| `ad_server_config` | String |  | Required. Immutable. Ad server related settings of the advertiser. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the advertiser. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not insertion orders and line items of the advertiser can spend their budgets and bid on inventory. * Accepted values are `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`, `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` and `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`. * If set to `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`, the advertiser will be deleted 30 days from when it was first scheduled for deletion. |
| `contains_eu_political_ads` | String |  | Optional. Whether this advertiser contains line items that serve European Union political ads. If this field is set to `DOES_NOT_CONTAIN_EU_POLITICAL_ADVERTISING`, then the following will happen: * Any new line items created under this advertiser will be assigned `DOES_NOT_CONTAIN_EU_POLITICAL_ADVERTISING` if not otherwise specified. * Any existing line items under this advertiser that do not have a set value be updated to `DOES_NOT_CONTAIN_EU_POLITICAL_ADVERTISING` within a day. |
| `general_config` | String |  | Required. General settings of the advertiser. |
| `creative_config` | String |  | Required. Creative related settings of the advertiser. |
| `prisma_enabled` | bool |  | Whether integration with Mediaocean (Prisma) is enabled. By enabling this, you agree to the following: On behalf of my company, I authorize Mediaocean (Prisma) to send budget segment plans to Google, and I authorize Google to send corresponding reporting and invoices from DV360 to Mediaocean for the purposes of budget planning, billing, and reconciliation for this advertiser. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the advertiser. |
| `integration_details` | String |  | Integration details of the advertiser. Only integrationCode is currently applicable to advertiser. Other fields of IntegrationDetails are not supported and will be ignored if provided. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `data_access_config` | String | Settings that control how advertiser data may be accessed. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the advertiser was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `serving_config` | String | Targeting settings related to ad serving of the advertiser. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser. Assigned by the system. |
| `partner_id` | String | Required. Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that the advertiser belongs to. |
| `billing_config` | String | Required. Billing related settings of the advertiser. |
| `ad_server_config` | String | Required. Immutable. Ad server related settings of the advertiser. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the advertiser. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `entity_status` | String | Required. Controls whether or not insertion orders and line items of the advertiser can spend their budgets and bid on inventory. * Accepted values are `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`, `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` and `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`. * If set to `ENTITY_STATUS_SCHEDULED_FOR_DELETION`, the advertiser will be deleted 30 days from when it was first scheduled for deletion. |
| `contains_eu_political_ads` | String | Optional. Whether this advertiser contains line items that serve European Union political ads. If this field is set to `DOES_NOT_CONTAIN_EU_POLITICAL_ADVERTISING`, then the following will happen: * Any new line items created under this advertiser will be assigned `DOES_NOT_CONTAIN_EU_POLITICAL_ADVERTISING` if not otherwise specified. * Any existing line items under this advertiser that do not have a set value be updated to `DOES_NOT_CONTAIN_EU_POLITICAL_ADVERTISING` within a day. |
| `general_config` | String | Required. General settings of the advertiser. |
| `creative_config` | String | Required. Creative related settings of the advertiser. |
| `prisma_enabled` | bool | Whether integration with Mediaocean (Prisma) is enabled. By enabling this, you agree to the following: On behalf of my company, I authorize Mediaocean (Prisma) to send budget segment plans to Google, and I authorize Google to send corresponding reporting and invoices from DV360 to Mediaocean for the purposes of budget planning, billing, and reconciliation for this advertiser. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the advertiser. |
| `integration_details` | String | Integration details of the advertiser. Only integrationCode is currently applicable to advertiser. Other fields of IntegrationDetails are not supported and will be ignored if provided. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create advertiser
advertiser = provider.displayvideo_api.Advertiser {
}

# Access advertiser outputs
advertiser_id = advertiser.id
advertiser_data_access_config = advertiser.data_access_config
advertiser_update_time = advertiser.update_time
advertiser_serving_config = advertiser.serving_config
advertiser_advertiser_id = advertiser.advertiser_id
advertiser_partner_id = advertiser.partner_id
advertiser_billing_config = advertiser.billing_config
advertiser_ad_server_config = advertiser.ad_server_config
advertiser_display_name = advertiser.display_name
advertiser_entity_status = advertiser.entity_status
advertiser_contains_eu_political_ads = advertiser.contains_eu_political_ads
advertiser_general_config = advertiser.general_config
advertiser_creative_config = advertiser.creative_config
advertiser_prisma_enabled = advertiser.prisma_enabled
advertiser_name = advertiser.name
advertiser_integration_details = advertiser.integration_details
```

### Sdfdownloadtask

Creates an SDF Download Task. Returns an Operation. An SDF Download Task is a long-running, asynchronous operation. The metadata type of this operation is SdfDownloadTaskMetadata. If the request is successful, the response type of the operation is SdfDownloadTask. The response will not include the download files, which must be retrieved with media.download. The state of operation can be retrieved with `sdfdownloadtasks.operations.get`. Any errors can be found in the error.message. Note that error.details is expected to be empty.

**Operations**: ✅ Create

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `parent_entity_filter` | String |  | Filters on selected file types. The entities in each file are filtered by a chosen set of filter entities. The filter entities must be the same type as, or a parent type of, the selected file types. |
| `version` | String |  | Required. The SDF version of the downloaded file. If set to `SDF_VERSION_UNSPECIFIED`, this will default to the version specified by the advertiser or partner identified by `root_id`. An advertiser inherits its SDF version from its partner unless configured otherwise. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | The ID of the partner to download SDF for. |
| `inventory_source_filter` | String |  | Filters on Inventory Sources by their IDs. |
| `id_filter` | String |  | Filters on entities by their entity IDs. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | The ID of the advertiser to download SDF for. |



#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create sdfdownloadtask
sdfdownloadtask = provider.displayvideo_api.Sdfdownloadtask {
}

```

---

### Ad_group_ad

Gets an ad group ad.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `name` | String | The resource name of the ad. |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the ad. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. |
| `display_video_source_ad` | String | Details of an ad sourced from a Display & Video 360 creative. |
| `non_skippable_ad` | String | Details of a [non-skippable short in-stream video ad](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216), between 6 and 15 seconds, used for reach marketing objectives. |
| `ad_group_id` | String | The unique ID of the ad group that the ad belongs to. *Caution*: Parent ad groups for Demand Gen ads are not currently retrieveable using `advertisers.adGroups.list` or `advertisers.adGroups.get`. Demand Gen ads can be identified by the absence of the `ad_details` union field. |
| `ad_group_ad_id` | String | The unique ID of the ad. Assigned by the system. |
| `masthead_ad` | String | Details of an [ad served on the YouTube Home feed](//support.google.com/google-ads/answer/9709826). |
| `video_discover_ad` | String | Details of an [ad promoting a video](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216) that shows in places of discovery. |
| `audio_ad` | String | Details of an [audio ad](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216) used for reach marketing objectives. |
| `bumper_ad` | String | Details of a [non-skippable short video ad](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216), equal to or less than 6 seconds, used for reach. |
| `ad_policy` | String | The policy approval status of the ad. |
| `entity_status` | String | The entity status of the ad. |
| `in_stream_ad` | String | Details of an [in-stream ad skippable after 5 seconds](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216), used for brand awareness or reach marketing objectives. |
| `ad_urls` | Vec<String> | List of URLs used by the ad. |
| `video_performance_ad` | String | Details of an [ad used in a video action campaign](//support.google.com/google-ads/answer/10147229) to drive actions to the business, service or product. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | The unique ID of the advertiser the ad belongs to. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access ad_group_ad outputs
ad_group_ad_id = ad_group_ad.id
ad_group_ad_name = ad_group_ad.name
ad_group_ad_display_name = ad_group_ad.display_name
ad_group_ad_display_video_source_ad = ad_group_ad.display_video_source_ad
ad_group_ad_non_skippable_ad = ad_group_ad.non_skippable_ad
ad_group_ad_ad_group_id = ad_group_ad.ad_group_id
ad_group_ad_ad_group_ad_id = ad_group_ad.ad_group_ad_id
ad_group_ad_masthead_ad = ad_group_ad.masthead_ad
ad_group_ad_video_discover_ad = ad_group_ad.video_discover_ad
ad_group_ad_audio_ad = ad_group_ad.audio_ad
ad_group_ad_bumper_ad = ad_group_ad.bumper_ad
ad_group_ad_ad_policy = ad_group_ad.ad_policy
ad_group_ad_entity_status = ad_group_ad.entity_status
ad_group_ad_in_stream_ad = ad_group_ad.in_stream_ad
ad_group_ad_ad_urls = ad_group_ad.ad_urls
ad_group_ad_video_performance_ad = ad_group_ad.video_performance_ad
ad_group_ad_advertiser_id = ad_group_ad.advertiser_id
```

### Site

Creates a site in a channel.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the site. |
| `url_or_app_id` | String |  | Required. The app ID or URL of the site. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `channel_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the parent channel in which the site will be created. |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | The ID of the partner that owns the parent channel. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `sites` | Vec<String> | The list of sites. This list will be absent if empty. |
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListSites` method to retrieve the next page of results. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create site
site = provider.displayvideo_api.Site {
    channel_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the parent channel in which the site will be created.
    partner_id = "value"  # The ID of the partner that owns the parent channel.
}

# Access site outputs
site_id = site.id
site_sites = site.sites
site_next_page_token = site.next_page_token
```

### Negative_keyword

Creates a negative keyword in a negative keyword list.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `keyword_value` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The negatively targeted keyword, for example `car insurance`. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. Maximum number of characters is 80. Maximum number of words is 10. Valid characters are restricted to ASCII characters only. The only URL-escaping permitted is for representing whitespace between words. Leading or trailing whitespace is ignored. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the negative keyword. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the parent negative keyword list belongs. |
| `negative_keyword_list_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the parent negative keyword list in which the negative keyword will be created. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `negative_keywords` | Vec<String> | The list of negative keywords. This list will be absent if empty. |
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListNegativeKeywords` method to retrieve the next page of results. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create negative_keyword
negative_keyword = provider.displayvideo_api.Negative_keyword {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the parent negative keyword list belongs.
    negative_keyword_list_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the parent negative keyword list in which the negative keyword will be created.
}

# Access negative_keyword outputs
negative_keyword_id = negative_keyword.id
negative_keyword_negative_keywords = negative_keyword.negative_keywords
negative_keyword_next_page_token = negative_keyword.next_page_token
```

### Channel

Creates a new channel. Returns the newly created channel if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `negatively_targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel negatively. |
| `channel_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the channel. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the channel. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | The ID of the advertiser that owns the channel. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | The ID of the partner that owns the channel. |
| `positively_targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel positively. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the channel. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | The ID of the partner that owns the created channel. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `negatively_targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel negatively. |
| `channel_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the channel. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the channel. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | The ID of the advertiser that owns the channel. |
| `partner_id` | String | The ID of the partner that owns the channel. |
| `positively_targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel positively. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the channel. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create channel

    partner_id = "value"  # The ID of the partner that owns the created channel.
}

# Access channel outputs
```

### Script

Creates a new custom bidding script. Returns the newly created script if successful. Requests creating a custom bidding script under an algorithm assigned to a line item will return an error.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `errors` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. Error details of a rejected custom bidding script. This field will only be populated when state is REJECTED. |
| `state` | String |  | Output only. The state of the custom bidding script. |
| `script` | String |  | The reference to the uploaded script file. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The time when the script was created. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm the script belongs to. |
| `custom_bidding_script_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding script. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding script. |
| `active` | bool |  | Output only. Whether the script is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the script. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `errors` | Vec<String> | Output only. Error details of a rejected custom bidding script. This field will only be populated when state is REJECTED. |
| `state` | String | Output only. The state of the custom bidding script. |
| `script` | String | The reference to the uploaded script file. |
| `create_time` | String | Output only. The time when the script was created. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm the script belongs to. |
| `custom_bidding_script_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding script. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding script. |
| `active` | bool | Output only. Whether the script is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create script
script = provider.displayvideo_api.Script {
    custom_bidding_algorithm_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the script.
}

# Access script outputs
script_id = script.id
script_errors = script.errors
script_state = script.state
script_script = script.script
script_create_time = script.create_time
script_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = script.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
script_custom_bidding_script_id = script.custom_bidding_script_id
script_name = script.name
script_active = script.active
```

### Custom_bidding_algorithm

Creates a new custom bidding algorithm. Returns the newly created custom bidding algorithm if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `model_details` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The details of custom bidding models for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the details of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `partner_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `model_details` | Vec<String> | Output only. The details of custom bidding models for each advertiser who has access. This field may only include the details of the queried advertiser if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `partner_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the partner that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of custom bidding algorithm. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Immutable. The unique ID of the advertiser that owns the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `shared_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of the advertisers who have access to this algorithm. If advertiser_id is set, this field will only consist of that value. This field will not be set if the algorithm [`owner`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms#CustomBiddingAlgorithm.FIELDS.oneof_owner) is a partner and is being retrieved using an advertiser [`accessor`](/display-video/api/reference/rest/v1/customBiddingAlgorithms/list#body.QUERY_PARAMETERS.oneof_accessor). |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the custom bidding algorithm. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `entity_status` | String | Controls whether or not the custom bidding algorithm can be used as a bidding strategy. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm. Assigned by the system. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create custom_bidding_algorithm
custom_bidding_algorithm = provider.displayvideo_api.Custom_bidding_algorithm {
}

# Access custom_bidding_algorithm outputs
custom_bidding_algorithm_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.id
custom_bidding_algorithm_model_details = custom_bidding_algorithm.model_details
custom_bidding_algorithm_partner_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.partner_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_type = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_type
custom_bidding_algorithm_advertiser_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.advertiser_id
custom_bidding_algorithm_shared_advertiser_ids = custom_bidding_algorithm.shared_advertiser_ids
custom_bidding_algorithm_display_name = custom_bidding_algorithm.display_name
custom_bidding_algorithm_entity_status = custom_bidding_algorithm.entity_status
custom_bidding_algorithm_name = custom_bidding_algorithm.name
custom_bidding_algorithm_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = custom_bidding_algorithm.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
```

If enabled, this Floodlight Activity generates a remarketing user list that is able to be used in targeting under the advertiser. |

### User

Creates a new user. Returns the newly created user if successful. This method has unique authentication requirements. Read the prerequisites in our [Managing Users guide](/display-video/api/guides/users/overview#prerequisites) before using this method. The "Try this method" feature does not work for this method.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the user. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `assigned_user_roles` | Vec<String> |  | The assigned user roles. Required in CreateUser. Output only in UpdateUser. Can only be updated through BulkEditAssignedUserRoles. |
| `email` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The email address used to identify the user. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the user. |
| `user_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the user. Assigned by the system. |
| `last_login_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the user last logged in DV360 UI. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the user. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `assigned_user_roles` | Vec<String> | The assigned user roles. Required in CreateUser. Output only in UpdateUser. Can only be updated through BulkEditAssignedUserRoles. |
| `email` | String | Required. Immutable. The email address used to identify the user. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the user. |
| `user_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the user. Assigned by the system. |
| `last_login_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the user last logged in DV360 UI. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create user
user = provider.displayvideo_api.User {
}

# Access user outputs
user_id = user.id
user_display_name = user.display_name
user_assigned_user_roles = user.assigned_user_roles
user_email = user.email
user_name = user.name
user_user_id = user.user_id
user_last_login_time = user.last_login_time
```

### Assigned_inventory_source

Creates an assignment between an inventory source and an inventory source group.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `inventory_source_id` | String |  | Required. The ID of the inventory source entity being targeted. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the assigned inventory source. |
| `assigned_inventory_source_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned inventory source. The ID is only unique within a given inventory source group. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `inventory_source_group_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the inventory source group to which the assignment will be assigned. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `assigned_inventory_sources` | Vec<String> | The list of assigned inventory sources. This list will be absent if empty. |
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListAssignedInventorySources` method to retrieve the next page of results. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create assigned_inventory_source
assigned_inventory_source = provider.displayvideo_api.Assigned_inventory_source {
    inventory_source_group_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the inventory source group to which the assignment will be assigned.
}

# Access assigned_inventory_source outputs
assigned_inventory_source_id = assigned_inventory_source.id
assigned_inventory_source_assigned_inventory_sources = assigned_inventory_source.assigned_inventory_sources
assigned_inventory_source_next_page_token = assigned_inventory_source.next_page_token
```

### Assigned_targeting_option

Assigns a targeting option to a partner. Returns the assigned targeting option if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `native_content_position_details` | String |  | Native content position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION`. |
| `audio_content_type_details` | String |  | Audio content type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIO_CONTENT_TYPE`. |
| `content_genre_details` | String |  | Content genre details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_GENRE`. |
| `poi_details` | String |  | POI details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_POI`. |
| `content_theme_exclusion_details` | String |  | Content theme details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_THEME_EXCLUSION`. Content theme are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level content theme exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude content theme in addition to advertiser exclusions. |
| `targeting_type` | String |  | Output only. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. |
| `channel_details` | String |  | Channel details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL`. |
| `language_details` | String |  | Language details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_LANGUAGE`. |
| `inventory_source_details` | String |  | Inventory source details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE`. |
| `omid_details` | String |  | Open Measurement enabled inventory details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_OMID`. |
| `app_category_details` | String |  | App category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_APP_CATEGORY`. |
| `video_player_size_details` | String |  | Video player size details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE`. |
| `assigned_targeting_option_id_alias` | String |  | Output only. An alias for the assigned_targeting_option_id. This value can be used in place of `assignedTargetingOptionId` when retrieving or deleting existing targeting. This field will only be supported for all assigned targeting options of the following targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT` * `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME` * `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_OMID` * `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS` * `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY` This field is also supported for line item assigned targeting options of the following targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION` |
| `day_and_time_details` | String |  | Day and time details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DAY_AND_TIME`. |
| `authorized_seller_status_details` | String |  | Authorized seller status details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUTHORIZED_SELLER_STATUS`. You can only target one authorized seller status option per resource. If a resource doesn't have an authorized seller status option, all authorized sellers indicated as DIRECT or RESELLER in the ads.txt file are targeted by default. |
| `business_chain_details` | String |  | Business chain details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`. |
| `digital_content_label_exclusion_details` | String |  | Digital content label details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION`. Digital content labels are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level digital content label exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude content labels in addition to advertiser exclusions, but can't override them. A line item won't serve if all the digital content labels are excluded. |
| `assigned_targeting_option_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned targeting option. The ID is only unique within a given resource and targeting type. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name for this assigned targeting option. |
| `browser_details` | String |  | Browser details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BROWSER`. |
| `on_screen_position_details` | String |  | On screen position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ON_SCREEN_POSITION`. |
| `session_position_details` | String |  | Session position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SESSION_POSITION`. |
| `url_details` | String |  | URL details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_URL`. |
| `category_details` | String |  | Category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CATEGORY`. Targeting a category will also target its subcategories. If a category is excluded from targeting and a subcategory is included, the exclusion will take precedence. |
| `device_type_details` | String |  | Device Type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE`. |
| `inheritance` | String |  | Output only. The inheritance status of the assigned targeting option. |
| `viewability_details` | String |  | Viewability details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY`. You can only target one viewability option per resource. |
| `app_details` | String |  | App details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_APP`. |
| `environment_details` | String |  | Environment details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT`. |
| `negative_keyword_list_details` | String |  | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NEGATIVE_KEYWORD_LIST`. A maximum of 4 negative keyword lists can be assigned to a resource. |
| `sub_exchange_details` | String |  | Sub-exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SUB_EXCHANGE`. |
| `content_outstream_position_details` | String |  | Content outstream position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION`. |
| `user_rewarded_content_details` | String |  | User rewarded content details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_USER_REWARDED_CONTENT`. |
| `carrier_and_isp_details` | String |  | Carrier and ISP details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CARRIER_AND_ISP`. |
| `device_make_model_details` | String |  | Device make and model details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_MAKE_MODEL`. |
| `inventory_source_group_details` | String |  | Inventory source group details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE_GROUP`. |
| `regional_location_list_details` | String |  | Regional location list details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_REGIONAL_LOCATION_LIST`. |
| `youtube_channel_details` | String |  | YouTube channel details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_YOUTUBE_CHANNEL`. |
| `youtube_video_details` | String |  | YouTube video details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_YOUTUBE_VIDEO`. |
| `household_income_details` | String |  | Household income details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME`. |
| `audience_group_details` | String |  | Audience targeting details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIENCE_GROUP`. You can only target one audience group option per resource. |
| `age_range_details` | String |  | Age range details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE`. |
| `keyword_details` | String |  | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_KEYWORD`. A maximum of 5000 direct negative keywords can be assigned to a resource. No limit on number of positive keywords that can be assigned. |
| `exchange_details` | String |  | Exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE`. |
| `content_stream_type_details` | String |  | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the TargetingType is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_STREAM_TYPE`. |
| `content_instream_position_details` | String |  | Content instream position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION`. |
| `operating_system_details` | String |  | Operating system details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_OPERATING_SYSTEM`. |
| `content_duration_details` | String |  | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_DURATION`. |
| `parental_status_details` | String |  | Parental status details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS`. |
| `proximity_location_list_details` | String |  | Proximity location list details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_PROXIMITY_LOCATION_LIST`. |
| `sensitive_category_exclusion_details` | String |  | Sensitive category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION`. Sensitive categories are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level sensitive category exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude sensitive categories in addition to advertiser exclusions, but can't override them. |
| `third_party_verifier_details` | String |  | Third party verification details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_THIRD_PARTY_VERIFIER`. |
| `geo_region_details` | String |  | Geographic region details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION`. |
| `gender_details` | String |  | Gender details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER`. |
| `targeting_type` | String | ✅ | Required. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. Supported targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL` |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the partner. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `native_content_position_details` | String | Native content position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION`. |
| `audio_content_type_details` | String | Audio content type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIO_CONTENT_TYPE`. |

Content theme are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level content theme exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude content theme in addition to advertiser exclusions. |
| `targeting_type` | String | Output only. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. |
| `channel_details` | String | Channel details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL`. |
| `language_details` | String | Language details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_LANGUAGE`. |
| `inventory_source_details` | String | Inventory source details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE`. |

| `assigned_targeting_option_id_alias` | String | Output only. An alias for the assigned_targeting_option_id. This value can be used in place of `assignedTargetingOptionId` when retrieving or deleting existing targeting. This field will only be supported for all assigned targeting options of the following targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT` * `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER` * `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME` * `TARGETING_TYPE_NATIVE_CONTENT_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_OMID` * `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS` * `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIDEO_PLAYER_SIZE` * `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY` This field is also supported for line item assigned targeting options of the following targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION` |
| `day_and_time_details` | String | Day and time details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DAY_AND_TIME`. |
| `authorized_seller_status_details` | String | Authorized seller status details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUTHORIZED_SELLER_STATUS`. You can only target one authorized seller status option per resource. If a resource doesn't have an authorized seller status option, all authorized sellers indicated as DIRECT or RESELLER in the ads.txt file are targeted by default. |
| `business_chain_details` | String | Business chain details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`. |
| `digital_content_label_exclusion_details` | String | Digital content label details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DIGITAL_CONTENT_LABEL_EXCLUSION`. Digital content labels are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level digital content label exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude content labels in addition to advertiser exclusions, but can't override them. A line item won't serve if all the digital content labels are excluded. |
| `assigned_targeting_option_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned targeting option. The ID is only unique within a given resource and targeting type. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name for this assigned targeting option. |
| `browser_details` | String | Browser details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BROWSER`. |
| `on_screen_position_details` | String | On screen position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ON_SCREEN_POSITION`. |
| `session_position_details` | String | Session position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SESSION_POSITION`. |
| `url_details` | String | URL details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_URL`. |
| `category_details` | String | Category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CATEGORY`. Targeting a category will also target its subcategories. If a category is excluded from targeting and a subcategory is included, the exclusion will take precedence. |
| `device_type_details` | String | Device Type details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_TYPE`. |
| `inheritance` | String | Output only. The inheritance status of the assigned targeting option. |
| `viewability_details` | String | Viewability details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_VIEWABILITY`. You can only target one viewability option per resource. |
| `app_details` | String | App details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_APP`. |
| `environment_details` | String | Environment details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_ENVIRONMENT`. |
| `negative_keyword_list_details` | String | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_NEGATIVE_KEYWORD_LIST`. A maximum of 4 negative keyword lists can be assigned to a resource. |
| `sub_exchange_details` | String | Sub-exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SUB_EXCHANGE`. |
| `content_outstream_position_details` | String | Content outstream position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_OUTSTREAM_POSITION`. |
| `user_rewarded_content_details` | String | User rewarded content details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_USER_REWARDED_CONTENT`. |
| `carrier_and_isp_details` | String | Carrier and ISP details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CARRIER_AND_ISP`. |
| `device_make_model_details` | String | Device make and model details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_DEVICE_MAKE_MODEL`. |
| `inventory_source_group_details` | String | Inventory source group details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_INVENTORY_SOURCE_GROUP`. |
| `regional_location_list_details` | String | Regional location list details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_REGIONAL_LOCATION_LIST`. |
| `youtube_channel_details` | String | YouTube channel details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_YOUTUBE_CHANNEL`. |
| `youtube_video_details` | String | YouTube video details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_YOUTUBE_VIDEO`. |
| `household_income_details` | String | Household income details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_HOUSEHOLD_INCOME`. |
| `audience_group_details` | String | Audience targeting details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AUDIENCE_GROUP`. You can only target one audience group option per resource. |
| `age_range_details` | String | Age range details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_AGE_RANGE`. |
| `keyword_details` | String | Keyword details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_KEYWORD`. A maximum of 5000 direct negative keywords can be assigned to a resource. No limit on number of positive keywords that can be assigned. |
| `exchange_details` | String | Exchange details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_EXCHANGE`. |
| `content_stream_type_details` | String | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the TargetingType is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_STREAM_TYPE`. |
| `content_instream_position_details` | String | Content instream position details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_INSTREAM_POSITION`. |
| `operating_system_details` | String | Operating system details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_OPERATING_SYSTEM`. |
| `content_duration_details` | String | Content duration details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_CONTENT_DURATION`. |
| `parental_status_details` | String | Parental status details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_PARENTAL_STATUS`. |
| `proximity_location_list_details` | String | Proximity location list details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_PROXIMITY_LOCATION_LIST`. |
| `sensitive_category_exclusion_details` | String | Sensitive category details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_SENSITIVE_CATEGORY_EXCLUSION`. Sensitive categories are targeting exclusions. Advertiser level sensitive category exclusions, if set, are always applied in serving (even though they aren't visible in resource settings). Resource settings can exclude sensitive categories in addition to advertiser exclusions, but can't override them. |
| `third_party_verifier_details` | String | Third party verification details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_THIRD_PARTY_VERIFIER`. |
| `geo_region_details` | String | Geographic region details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION`. |
| `gender_details` | String | Gender details. This field will be populated when the targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GENDER`. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create assigned_targeting_option
assigned_targeting_option = provider.displayvideo_api.Assigned_targeting_option {
    targeting_type = "value"  # Required. Identifies the type of this assigned targeting option. Supported targeting types: * `TARGETING_TYPE_CHANNEL`
    partner_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the partner.
}

# Access assigned_targeting_option outputs
assigned_targeting_option_id = assigned_targeting_option.id
assigned_targeting_option_native_content_position_details = assigned_targeting_option.native_content_position_details
assigned_targeting_option_audio_content_type_details = assigned_targeting_option.audio_content_type_details
```
