### Channel

Creates a new channel. Returns the newly created channel if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the channel. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `positively_targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel positively. |
| `channel_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the channel. Assigned by the system. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | The ID of the advertiser that owns the channel. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the channel. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | The ID of the partner that owns the channel. |
| `negatively_targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel negatively. |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | The ID of the partner that owns the created channel. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the channel. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `positively_targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel positively. |
| `channel_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the channel. Assigned by the system. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | The ID of the advertiser that owns the channel. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the channel. |
| `partner_id` | String | The ID of the partner that owns the channel. |
| `negatively_targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this channel negatively. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create channel
channel = provider.displayvideo_api.Channel {
    partner_id = "value"  # The ID of the partner that owns the created channel.
}

# Access channel outputs
channel_id = channel.id
channel_display_name = channel.display_name
channel_positively_targeted_line_item_count = channel.positively_targeted_line_item_count
channel_channel_id = channel.channel_id
channel_advertiser_id = channel.advertiser_id
channel_name = channel.name
channel_partner_id = channel.partner_id
channel_negatively_targeted_line_item_count = channel.negatively_targeted_line_item_count
```

---


### Assigned_location

Creates an assignment between a location and a location list.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `targeting_option_id` | String |  | Required. The ID of the targeting option assigned to the location list. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the assigned location. |
| `assigned_location_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the assigned location. The ID is only unique within a location list. It may be reused in other contexts. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the location list belongs. |
| `location_list_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the location list for which the assignment will be created. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `assigned_locations` | Vec<String> | The list of assigned locations. This list will be absent if empty. |
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListAssignedLocations` method to retrieve the next page of results. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create assigned_location
assigned_location = provider.displayvideo_api.Assigned_location {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the location list belongs.
    location_list_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the location list for which the assignment will be created.
}

# Access assigned_location outputs
assigned_location_id = assigned_location.id
assigned_location_assigned_locations = assigned_location.assigned_locations
assigned_location_next_page_token = assigned_location.next_page_token
```

---


### Asset

Uploads an asset. Returns the ID of the newly uploaded asset if successful. The asset file size should be no more than 10 MB for images, 200 MB for ZIP files, and 1 GB for videos. Must be used within the [multipart media upload process](/display-video/api/guides/how-tos/upload#multipart). Examples using provided client libraries can be found in our [Creating Creatives guide](/display-video/api/guides/creating-creatives/overview#upload_an_asset).

**Operations**: ✅ Create

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `filename` | String |  | Required. The filename of the asset, including the file extension. The filename must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the advertiser this asset belongs to. |



#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create asset
asset = provider.displayvideo_api.Asset {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the advertiser this asset belongs to.
}

```

---


### Site

Creates a site in a channel.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `url_or_app_id` | String |  | Required. The app ID or URL of the site. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum length of 240 bytes. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the site. |
| `channel_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the parent channel in which the site will be created. |
| `partner_id` | String | ✅ | The ID of the partner that owns the parent channel. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListSites` method to retrieve the next page of results. |
| `sites` | Vec<String> | The list of sites. This list will be absent if empty. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create site
site = provider.displayvideo_api.Site {
    channel_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the parent channel in which the site will be created.
    partner_id = "value"  # The ID of the partner that owns the parent channel.
}

# Access site outputs
site_id = site.id
site_next_page_token = site.next_page_token
site_sites = site.sites
```

---


### Creative

Creates a new creative. Returns the newly created creative if successful. A ["Standard" user role](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/2723011) or greater for the parent advertiser or partner is required to make this request.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `notes` | String |  | Optional. User notes for this creative. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a length of no more than 20,000 characters. |
| `creative_type` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The type of the creative. |
| `ogg_audio` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports OGG. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `dimensions` | String |  | Required. Primary dimensions of the creative. Applicable to all creative types. The value of width_pixels and height_pixels defaults to `0` when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `cm_placement_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the Campaign Manager 360 placement associated with the creative. This field is only applicable for creatives that are synced from Campaign Manager. |
| `counter_events` | Vec<String> |  | Optional. Counter events for a rich media creative. Counters track the number of times that a user interacts with any part of a rich media creative in a specified way (mouse-overs, mouse-outs, clicks, taps, data loading, keyboard entries, etc.). Any event that can be captured in the creative can be recorded as a counter. Leave it empty or unset for creatives containing image assets only. |
| `line_item_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. The IDs of the line items this creative is associated with. To associate a creative to a line item, use LineItem.creative_ids instead. |
| `media_duration` | String |  | Output only. Media duration of the creative. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` |
| `js_tracker_url` | String |  | Optional. JavaScript measurement URL from supported third-party verification providers (ComScore, DoubleVerify, IAS, Moat). HTML script tags are not supported. This field is only writeable in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `third_party_tag` | String |  | Optional. The original third-party tag used for the creative. Required and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `tracker_urls` | Vec<String> |  | Optional. Tracking URLs for analytics providers or third-party ad technology vendors. The URLs must start with `https:` (except on inventory that doesn't require SSL compliance). If using macros in your URL, use only macros supported by Display & Video 360. Standard URLs only, no IMG or SCRIPT tags. This field is only writeable in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `vpaid` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires VPAID (Digital Video Player-Ad Interface). Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `companion_creative_ids` | Vec<String> |  | Optional. The IDs of companion creatives for a video creative. You can assign existing display creatives (with image or HTML5 assets) to serve surrounding the publisher's video player. Companions display around the video player while the video is playing and remain after the video has completed. Creatives contain additional dimensions can not be companion creatives. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the creative. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `html5_video` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires HTML5 Video support. Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `progress_offset` | String |  | Optional. Amount of time to play the video before counting a view. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `skippable` | bool |  | Optional. Whether the user can choose to skip a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `timer_events` | Vec<String> |  | Optional. Timer custom events for a rich media creative. Timers track the time during which a user views and interacts with a specified part of a rich media creative. A creative can have multiple timer events, each timed independently. Leave it empty or unset for creatives containing image assets only. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to. |
| `additional_dimensions` | Vec<String> |  | Optional. Additional dimensions. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_LIGHTBOX` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` If this field is specified, width_pixels and height_pixels are both required and must be greater than or equal to 0. |
| `require_mraid` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates that the creative requires MRAID (Mobile Rich Media Ad Interface Definitions system). Set this if the creative relies on mobile gestures for interactivity, such as swiping or tapping. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `review_status` | String |  | Output only. The current status of the creative review process. |
| `creative_attributes` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. A list of attributes of the creative that is generated by the system. |
| `hosting_source` | String |  | Required. Indicates where the creative is hosted. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the creative was last updated, either by the user or system (e.g. creative review). Assigned by the system. |
| `transcodes` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. Audio/Video transcodes. Display & Video 360 transcodes the main asset into a number of alternative versions that use different file formats or have different properties (resolution, audio bit rate, and video bit rate), each designed for specific video players or bandwidths. These transcodes give a publisher's system more options to choose from for each impression on your video and ensures that the appropriate file serves based on the viewer’s connection and screen size. This field is only supported in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `require_html5` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates that the creative relies on HTML5 to render properly. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `universal_ad_id` | String |  | Optional. An optional creative identifier provided by a registry that is unique across all platforms. Universal Ad ID is part of the VAST 4.0 standard. It can be modified after the creative is created. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `entity_status` | String |  | Required. Controls whether or not the creative can serve. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` * `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` |
| `dynamic` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates whether the creative is dynamic. |
| `expanding_direction` | String |  | Optional. Specifies the expanding direction of the creative. Required and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `assets` | Vec<String> |  | Required. Assets associated to this creative. |
| `third_party_urls` | Vec<String> |  | Optional. Tracking URLs from third parties to track interactions with a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `vast_tag_url` | String |  | Optional. The URL of the VAST tag for a third-party VAST tag creative. Required and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `expand_on_hover` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates the creative will automatically expand on hover. Optional and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `require_ping_for_attribution` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates that the creative will wait for a return ping for attribution. Only valid when using a Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad with a third-party ad server parameter and the ${DC_DBM_TOKEN} macro. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives or third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `oba_icon` | String |  | Optional. Specifies the OBA icon for a video creative. This field is only supported in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `cm_tracking_ad` | String |  | Optional. The Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad associated with the creative. Optional for the following creative_type when created by an advertiser that uses both Campaign Manager 360 and third-party ad serving: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` Output only for other cases. |
| `skip_offset` | String |  | Optional. Amount of time to play the video before the skip button appears. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `creative_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the creative. Assigned by the system. |
| `exit_events` | Vec<String> |  | Required. Exit events for this creative. An exit (also known as a click tag) is any area in your creative that someone can click or tap to open an advertiser's landing page. Every creative must include at least one exit. You can add an exit to your creative in any of the following ways: * Use Google Web Designer's tap area. * Define a JavaScript variable called "clickTag". * Use the Enabler (Enabler.exit()) to track exits in rich media formats. |
| `appended_tag` | String |  | Optional. Third-party HTML tracking tag to be appended to the creative tag. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the creative. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the creative was created. Assigned by the system. |
| `integration_code` | String |  | Optional. ID information used to link this creative to an external system. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a length of no more than 10,000 characters. |
| `ias_campaign_monitoring` | bool |  | Optional. Indicates whether Integral Ad Science (IAS) campaign monitoring is enabled. To enable this for the creative, make sure the Advertiser.creative_config.ias_client_id has been set to your IAS client ID. |
| `mp3_audio` | bool |  | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports MP3. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `notes` | String | Optional. User notes for this creative. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a length of no more than 20,000 characters. |
| `creative_type` | String | Required. Immutable. The type of the creative. |
| `ogg_audio` | bool | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports OGG. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `dimensions` | String | Required. Primary dimensions of the creative. Applicable to all creative types. The value of width_pixels and height_pixels defaults to `0` when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `cm_placement_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the Campaign Manager 360 placement associated with the creative. This field is only applicable for creatives that are synced from Campaign Manager. |
| `counter_events` | Vec<String> | Optional. Counter events for a rich media creative. Counters track the number of times that a user interacts with any part of a rich media creative in a specified way (mouse-overs, mouse-outs, clicks, taps, data loading, keyboard entries, etc.). Any event that can be captured in the creative can be recorded as a counter. Leave it empty or unset for creatives containing image assets only. |
| `line_item_ids` | Vec<String> | Output only. The IDs of the line items this creative is associated with. To associate a creative to a line item, use LineItem.creative_ids instead. |
| `media_duration` | String | Output only. Media duration of the creative. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` |
| `js_tracker_url` | String | Optional. JavaScript measurement URL from supported third-party verification providers (ComScore, DoubleVerify, IAS, Moat). HTML script tags are not supported. This field is only writeable in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `third_party_tag` | String | Optional. The original third-party tag used for the creative. Required and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `tracker_urls` | Vec<String> | Optional. Tracking URLs for analytics providers or third-party ad technology vendors. The URLs must start with `https:` (except on inventory that doesn't require SSL compliance). If using macros in your URL, use only macros supported by Display & Video 360. Standard URLs only, no IMG or SCRIPT tags. This field is only writeable in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `vpaid` | bool | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires VPAID (Digital Video Player-Ad Interface). Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `companion_creative_ids` | Vec<String> | Optional. The IDs of companion creatives for a video creative. You can assign existing display creatives (with image or HTML5 assets) to serve surrounding the publisher's video player. Companions display around the video player while the video is playing and remain after the video has completed. Creatives contain additional dimensions can not be companion creatives. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the creative. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `html5_video` | bool | Output only. Indicates the third-party VAST tag creative requires HTML5 Video support. Output only and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `progress_offset` | String | Optional. Amount of time to play the video before counting a view. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `skippable` | bool | Optional. Whether the user can choose to skip a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `timer_events` | Vec<String> | Optional. Timer custom events for a rich media creative. Timers track the time during which a user views and interacts with a specified part of a rich media creative. A creative can have multiple timer events, each timed independently. Leave it empty or unset for creatives containing image assets only. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to. |
| `additional_dimensions` | Vec<String> | Optional. Additional dimensions. Applicable when creative_type is one of: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_LIGHTBOX` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_PUBLISHER_HOSTED` If this field is specified, width_pixels and height_pixels are both required and must be greater than or equal to 0. |
| `require_mraid` | bool | Optional. Indicates that the creative requires MRAID (Mobile Rich Media Ad Interface Definitions system). Set this if the creative relies on mobile gestures for interactivity, such as swiping or tapping. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `review_status` | String | Output only. The current status of the creative review process. |
| `creative_attributes` | Vec<String> | Output only. A list of attributes of the creative that is generated by the system. |
| `hosting_source` | String | Required. Indicates where the creative is hosted. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the creative was last updated, either by the user or system (e.g. creative review). Assigned by the system. |
| `transcodes` | Vec<String> | Output only. Audio/Video transcodes. Display & Video 360 transcodes the main asset into a number of alternative versions that use different file formats or have different properties (resolution, audio bit rate, and video bit rate), each designed for specific video players or bandwidths. These transcodes give a publisher's system more options to choose from for each impression on your video and ensures that the appropriate file serves based on the viewer’s connection and screen size. This field is only supported in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |
| `require_html5` | bool | Optional. Indicates that the creative relies on HTML5 to render properly. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `universal_ad_id` | String | Optional. An optional creative identifier provided by a registry that is unique across all platforms. Universal Ad ID is part of the VAST 4.0 standard. It can be modified after the creative is created. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `entity_status` | String | Required. Controls whether or not the creative can serve. Accepted values are: * `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE` * `ENTITY_STATUS_ARCHIVED` * `ENTITY_STATUS_PAUSED` |
| `dynamic` | bool | Output only. Indicates whether the creative is dynamic. |
| `expanding_direction` | String | Optional. Specifies the expanding direction of the creative. Required and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `assets` | Vec<String> | Required. Assets associated to this creative. |
| `third_party_urls` | Vec<String> | Optional. Tracking URLs from third parties to track interactions with a video creative. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_VIDEO` |
| `vast_tag_url` | String | Optional. The URL of the VAST tag for a third-party VAST tag creative. Required and only valid for third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `expand_on_hover` | bool | Optional. Indicates the creative will automatically expand on hover. Optional and only valid for third-party expandable creatives. Third-party expandable creatives are creatives with following hosting source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` |
| `require_ping_for_attribution` | bool | Optional. Indicates that the creative will wait for a return ping for attribution. Only valid when using a Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad with a third-party ad server parameter and the ${DC_DBM_TOKEN} macro. Optional and only valid for third-party tag creatives or third-party VAST tag creatives. Third-party tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_STANDARD` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_EXPANDABLE` Third-party VAST tag creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `oba_icon` | String | Optional. Specifies the OBA icon for a video creative. This field is only supported in the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `cm_tracking_ad` | String | Optional. The Campaign Manager 360 tracking ad associated with the creative. Optional for the following creative_type when created by an advertiser that uses both Campaign Manager 360 and third-party ad serving: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE` * `CREATIVE_TYPE_NATIVE_SITE_SQUARE` Output only for other cases. |
| `skip_offset` | String | Optional. Amount of time to play the video before the skip button appears. This field is required when skippable is true. This field is only supported for the following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_VIDEO` |
| `creative_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the creative. Assigned by the system. |
| `exit_events` | Vec<String> | Required. Exit events for this creative. An exit (also known as a click tag) is any area in your creative that someone can click or tap to open an advertiser's landing page. Every creative must include at least one exit. You can add an exit to your creative in any of the following ways: * Use Google Web Designer's tap area. * Define a JavaScript variable called "clickTag". * Use the Enabler (Enabler.exit()) to track exits in rich media formats. |
| `appended_tag` | String | Optional. Third-party HTML tracking tag to be appended to the creative tag. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the creative. |
| `create_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the creative was created. Assigned by the system. |
| `integration_code` | String | Optional. ID information used to link this creative to an external system. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a length of no more than 10,000 characters. |
| `ias_campaign_monitoring` | bool | Optional. Indicates whether Integral Ad Science (IAS) campaign monitoring is enabled. To enable this for the creative, make sure the Advertiser.creative_config.ias_client_id has been set to your IAS client ID. |
| `mp3_audio` | bool | Output only. Indicates the third-party audio creative supports MP3. Output only and only valid for third-party audio creatives. Third-party audio creatives are creatives with following hosting_source: * `HOSTING_SOURCE_THIRD_PARTY` combined with following creative_type: * `CREATIVE_TYPE_AUDIO` |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create creative
creative = provider.displayvideo_api.Creative {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the creative belongs to.
}

# Access creative outputs
creative_id = creative.id
creative_notes = creative.notes
creative_creative_type = creative.creative_type
creative_ogg_audio = creative.ogg_audio
creative_dimensions = creative.dimensions
creative_cm_placement_id = creative.cm_placement_id
creative_counter_events = creative.counter_events
creative_line_item_ids = creative.line_item_ids
creative_media_duration = creative.media_duration
creative_js_tracker_url = creative.js_tracker_url
creative_third_party_tag = creative.third_party_tag
creative_tracker_urls = creative.tracker_urls
creative_vpaid = creative.vpaid
creative_companion_creative_ids = creative.companion_creative_ids
creative_display_name = creative.display_name
creative_html5_video = creative.html5_video
creative_progress_offset = creative.progress_offset
creative_skippable = creative.skippable
creative_timer_events = creative.timer_events
creative_advertiser_id = creative.advertiser_id
creative_additional_dimensions = creative.additional_dimensions
creative_require_mraid = creative.require_mraid
creative_review_status = creative.review_status
creative_creative_attributes = creative.creative_attributes
creative_hosting_source = creative.hosting_source
creative_update_time = creative.update_time
creative_transcodes = creative.transcodes
creative_require_html5 = creative.require_html5
creative_universal_ad_id = creative.universal_ad_id
creative_entity_status = creative.entity_status
creative_dynamic = creative.dynamic
creative_expanding_direction = creative.expanding_direction
creative_assets = creative.assets
creative_third_party_urls = creative.third_party_urls
creative_vast_tag_url = creative.vast_tag_url
creative_expand_on_hover = creative.expand_on_hover
creative_require_ping_for_attribution = creative.require_ping_for_attribution
creative_oba_icon = creative.oba_icon
creative_cm_tracking_ad = creative.cm_tracking_ad
creative_skip_offset = creative.skip_offset
creative_creative_id = creative.creative_id
creative_exit_events = creative.exit_events
creative_appended_tag = creative.appended_tag
creative_name = creative.name
creative_create_time = creative.create_time
creative_integration_code = creative.integration_code
creative_ias_campaign_monitoring = creative.ias_campaign_monitoring
creative_mp3_audio = creative.mp3_audio
```

### Negative_keyword_list

Creates a new negative keyword list. Returns the newly created negative keyword list if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `targeted_line_item_count` | String |  | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this negative keyword list. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the negative keyword list belongs to. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the negative keyword list. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. |
| `negative_keyword_list_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the negative keyword list. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the negative keyword list. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the negative keyword list will belong. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `targeted_line_item_count` | String | Output only. Number of line items that are directly targeting this negative keyword list. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the advertiser the negative keyword list belongs to. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the negative keyword list. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. |
| `negative_keyword_list_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the negative keyword list. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the negative keyword list. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create negative_keyword_list
negative_keyword_list = provider.displayvideo_api.Negative_keyword_list {
    advertiser_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the DV360 advertiser to which the negative keyword list will belong.
}

# Access negative_keyword_list outputs
negative_keyword_list_id = negative_keyword_list.id
negative_keyword_list_targeted_line_item_count = negative_keyword_list.targeted_line_item_count
negative_keyword_list_advertiser_id = negative_keyword_list.advertiser_id
negative_keyword_list_display_name = negative_keyword_list.display_name
negative_keyword_list_negative_keyword_list_id = negative_keyword_list.negative_keyword_list_id
negative_keyword_list_name = negative_keyword_list.name
```

---


### Rule

Creates a new rules resource. Returns the newly created rules resource if successful. Requests creating a custom bidding rules resource under an algorithm assigned to a line item will return an error.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `active` | bool |  | Output only. Whether the rules resource is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm that the rules resource belongs to. |
| `error` | String |  | Output only. Error code of the rejected rules resource. This field will only be populated when the state is `REJECTED`. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the rules resource. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The time when the rules resource was created. |
| `rules` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The reference to the uploaded AlgorithmRules file. |
| `state` | String |  | Output only. The state of the rules resource. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the rules resource. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the rules resource. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `active` | bool | Output only. Whether the rules resource is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm that the rules resource belongs to. |
| `error` | String | Output only. Error code of the rejected rules resource. This field will only be populated when the state is `REJECTED`. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the rules resource. |
| `create_time` | String | Output only. The time when the rules resource was created. |
| `rules` | String | Required. Immutable. The reference to the uploaded AlgorithmRules file. |
| `state` | String | Output only. The state of the rules resource. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the rules resource. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create rule
rule = provider.displayvideo_api.Rule {
    custom_bidding_algorithm_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the rules resource.
}

# Access rule outputs
rule_id = rule.id
rule_active = rule.active
rule_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = rule.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
rule_error = rule.error
rule_name = rule.name
rule_create_time = rule.create_time
rule_rules = rule.rules
rule_state = rule.state
rule_custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id = rule.custom_bidding_algorithm_rules_id
```

---


### Media

Uploads media. Upload is supported on the URI `/upload/media/{resource_name=**}?upload_type=media.` **Note**: Upload requests will not be successful without including `upload_type=media` query string.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `resource_name` | String |  | Name of the media resource. |
| `resource_name` | String | ✅ | Name of the media that is being downloaded. See ReadRequest.resource_name. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `resource_name` | String | Name of the media resource. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create media
media = provider.displayvideo_api.Media {
    resource_name = "value"  # Name of the media that is being downloaded. See ReadRequest.resource_name.
}

# Access media outputs
media_id = media.id
media_resource_name = media.resource_name
```

---


### Floodlight_group

Gets a Floodlight group.

**Operations**: ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `active_view_config` | String |  | The Active View video viewability metric configuration for the Floodlight group. |
| `custom_variables` | HashMap<String, String> |  | User-defined custom variables owned by the Floodlight group. Use custom Floodlight variables to create reporting data that is tailored to your unique business needs. Custom Floodlight variables use the keys `U1=`, `U2=`, and so on, and can take any values that you choose to pass to them. You can use them to track virtually any type of data that you collect about your customers, such as the genre of movie that a customer purchases, the country to which the item is shipped, and so on. Custom Floodlight variables may not be used to pass any data that could be used or recognized as personally identifiable information (PII). Example: `custom_variables { fields { "U1": value { number_value: 123.4 }, "U2": value { string_value: "MyVariable2" }, "U3": value { string_value: "MyVariable3" } } }` Acceptable values for keys are "U1" through "U100", inclusive. String values must be less than 64 characters long, and cannot contain the following characters: `"<>`. |
| `web_tag_type` | String |  | Required. The web tag type enabled for the Floodlight group. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the Floodlight group. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the Floodlight group. |
| `lookback_window` | String |  | Required. The lookback window for the Floodlight group. Both click_days and impression_days are required. Acceptable values for both are `0` to `90`, inclusive. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String | ✅ | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `active_view_config` | String | The Active View video viewability metric configuration for the Floodlight group. |
| `custom_variables` | HashMap<String, String> | User-defined custom variables owned by the Floodlight group. Use custom Floodlight variables to create reporting data that is tailored to your unique business needs. Custom Floodlight variables use the keys `U1=`, `U2=`, and so on, and can take any values that you choose to pass to them. You can use them to track virtually any type of data that you collect about your customers, such as the genre of movie that a customer purchases, the country to which the item is shipped, and so on. Custom Floodlight variables may not be used to pass any data that could be used or recognized as personally identifiable information (PII). Example: `custom_variables { fields { "U1": value { number_value: 123.4 }, "U2": value { string_value: "MyVariable2" }, "U3": value { string_value: "MyVariable3" } } }` Acceptable values for keys are "U1" through "U100", inclusive. String values must be less than 64 characters long, and cannot contain the following characters: `"<>`. |
| `web_tag_type` | String | Required. The web tag type enabled for the Floodlight group. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the Floodlight group. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the Floodlight group. |
| `lookback_window` | String | Required. The lookback window for the Floodlight group. Both click_days and impression_days are required. Acceptable values for both are `0` to `90`, inclusive. |
| `floodlight_group_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the Floodlight group. Assigned by the system. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider

    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access floodlight_group outputs

floodlight_group_active_view_config = floodlight_group.active_view_config
floodlight_group_custom_variables = floodlight_group.custom_variables
floodlight_group_web_tag_type = floodlight_group.web_tag_type
floodlight_group_name = floodlight_group.name
floodlight_group_display_name = floodlight_group.display_name
floodlight_group_lookback_window = floodlight_group.lookback_window
floodlight_group_floodlight_group_id = floodlight_group.floodlight_group_id
```

### Sdfdownloadtask

Creates an SDF Download Task. Returns an Operation. An SDF Download Task is a long-running, asynchronous operation. The metadata type of this operation is SdfDownloadTaskMetadata. If the request is successful, the response type of the operation is SdfDownloadTask. The response will not include the download files, which must be retrieved with media.download. The state of operation can be retrieved with `sdfdownloadtasks.operations.get`. Any errors can be found in the error.message. Note that error.details is expected to be empty.

**Operations**: ✅ Create

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `version` | String |  | Required. The SDF version of the downloaded file. If set to `SDF_VERSION_UNSPECIFIED`, this will default to the version specified by the advertiser or partner identified by `root_id`. An advertiser inherits its SDF version from its partner unless configured otherwise. |
| `inventory_source_filter` | String |  | Filters on Inventory Sources by their IDs. |
| `id_filter` | String |  | Filters on entities by their entity IDs. |
| `partner_id` | String |  | The ID of the partner to download SDF for. |
| `parent_entity_filter` | String |  | Filters on selected file types. The entities in each file are filtered by a chosen set of filter entities. The filter entities must be the same type as, or a parent type of, the selected file types. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | The ID of the advertiser to download SDF for. |



#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create sdfdownloadtask
sdfdownloadtask = provider.displayvideo_api.Sdfdownloadtask {
}

```

---


### Operation

Gets the latest state of an asynchronous SDF download task operation. Clients should poll this method at intervals of 30 seconds.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `done` | bool | If the value is `false`, it means the operation is still in progress. If `true`, the operation is completed, and either `error` or `response` is available. |
| `response` | HashMap<String, String> | The normal, successful response of the operation. If the original method returns no data on success, such as `Delete`, the response is `google.protobuf.Empty`. If the original method is standard `Get`/`Create`/`Update`, the response should be the resource. For other methods, the response should have the type `XxxResponse`, where `Xxx` is the original method name. For example, if the original method name is `TakeSnapshot()`, the inferred response type is `TakeSnapshotResponse`. |
| `name` | String | The server-assigned name, which is only unique within the same service that originally returns it. If you use the default HTTP mapping, the `name` should be a resource name ending with `operations/{unique_id}`. |
| `metadata` | HashMap<String, String> | Service-specific metadata associated with the operation. It typically contains progress information and common metadata such as create time. Some services might not provide such metadata. Any method that returns a long-running operation should document the metadata type, if any. |
| `error` | String | The error result of the operation in case of failure or cancellation. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access operation outputs
operation_id = operation.id
operation_done = operation.done
operation_response = operation.response
operation_name = operation.name
operation_metadata = operation.metadata
operation_error = operation.error
```

### First_and_third_party_audience

Creates a FirstAndThirdPartyAudience. Only supported for the following audience_type: * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID`

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `first_and_third_party_audience_type` | String |  | Whether the audience is a first or third party audience. |
| `contact_info_list` | String |  | Input only. A list of contact information to define the initial audience members. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` |
| `display_desktop_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated desktop audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `first_and_third_party_audience_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the first and third party audience. Assigned by the system. |
| `audience_source` | String |  | Output only. The source of the audience. |
| `youtube_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for YouTube network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `description` | String |  | The user-provided description of the audience. Only applicable to first party audiences. |
| `audience_type` | String |  | The type of the audience. |
| `gmail_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for Gmail network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `display_mobile_web_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated mobile web audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |
| `membership_duration_days` | String |  | The duration in days that an entry remains in the audience after the qualifying event. The set value must be greater than 0 and less than or equal to 540. Only applicable to first party audiences. This field is required if one of the following audience_type is used: * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_CONTACT_INFO` * `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `display_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for the Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only returned in GET request. |
| `app_id` | String |  | The app_id matches with the type of the mobile_device_ids being uploaded. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `display_name` | String |  | The display name of the first and third party audience. |
| `mobile_device_id_list` | String |  | Input only. A list of mobile device IDs to define the initial audience members. Only applicable to audience_type `CUSTOMER_MATCH_DEVICE_ID` |
| `active_display_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated audience size for the Display network in the past month. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only returned in GET request. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the first and third party audience. |
| `display_mobile_app_audience_size` | String |  | Output only. The estimated mobile app audience size in Display network. If the size is less than 1000, the number will be hidden and 0 will be returned due to privacy reasons. Otherwise, the number will be rounded off to two significant digits. Only applicable to first party audiences. Only returned in GET request. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `first_and_third_party_audience_type` | String | Whether the audience is a first or third party audience. |

### Targeting_option

Searches for targeting options of a given type based on the given search terms.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `business_chain_search_terms` | String |  | Search terms for Business Chain targeting options. Can only be used when targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`. |
| `geo_region_search_terms` | String |  | Search terms for geo region targeting options. Can only be used when targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION`. |
| `advertiser_id` | String |  | Required. The Advertiser this request is being made in the context of. |
| `page_token` | String |  | A token identifying a page of results the server should return. Typically, this is the value of next_page_token returned from the previous call to `SearchTargetingOptions` method. If not specified, the first page of results will be returned. |
| `poi_search_terms` | String |  | Search terms for POI targeting options. Can only be used when targeting_type is `TARGETING_TYPE_POI`. |
| `page_size` | i64 |  | Requested page size. Must be between `1` and `200`. If unspecified will default to `100`. Returns error code `INVALID_ARGUMENT` if an invalid value is specified. |
| `targeting_type` | String | ✅ | Required. The type of targeting options to retrieve. Accepted values are: * `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_POI` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN` |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `content_genre_details` | String | Content genre resource details. |
| `device_make_model_details` | String | Device make and model resource details. |
| `authorized_seller_status_details` | String | Authorized seller status resource details. |
| `business_chain_details` | String | Business chain resource details. |
| `native_content_position_details` | String | Native content position details. |
| `omid_details` | String | Open Measurement enabled inventory details. |
| `age_range_details` | String | Age range details. |
| `category_details` | String | Category resource details. |
| `sensitive_category_details` | String | Sensitive Category details. |
| `content_duration_details` | String | Content duration resource details. |
| `poi_details` | String | POI resource details. |
| `environment_details` | String | Environment details. |
| `sub_exchange_details` | String | Sub-exchange details. |
| `digital_content_label_details` | String | Digital content label details. |
| `content_theme_details` | String | Content theme details. |
| `content_instream_position_details` | String | Content instream position details. |
| `geo_region_details` | String | Geographic region resource details. |
| `gender_details` | String | Gender details. |
| `app_category_details` | String | App category details. |
| `device_type_details` | String | Device type details. |
| `on_screen_position_details` | String | On screen position details. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name for this targeting option. |
| `video_player_size_details` | String | Video player size details. |
| `viewability_details` | String | Viewability resource details. |
| `household_income_details` | String | Household income details. |
| `user_rewarded_content_details` | String | User rewarded content details. |
| `content_stream_type_details` | String | Content stream type resource details. |
| `carrier_and_isp_details` | String | Carrier and ISP details. |
| `content_outstream_position_details` | String | Content outstream position details. |
| `operating_system_details` | String | Operating system resources details. |
| `audio_content_type_details` | String | Audio content type details. |
| `browser_details` | String | Browser details. |
| `exchange_details` | String | Exchange details. |
| `language_details` | String | Language resource details. |
| `targeting_option_id` | String | Output only. A unique identifier for this targeting option. The tuple {`targeting_type`, `targeting_option_id`} will be unique. |
| `parental_status_details` | String | Parental status details. |
| `targeting_type` | String | Output only. The type of this targeting option. |

# Initialize provider

    project = "my-project-id"
}

    targeting_type = "value"  # Required. The type of targeting options to retrieve. Accepted values are: * `TARGETING_TYPE_GEO_REGION` * `TARGETING_TYPE_POI` * `TARGETING_TYPE_BUSINESS_CHAIN`

### Inventory_source_group

Creates a new inventory source group. Returns the newly created inventory source group if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update ✅ Delete

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `inventory_source_group_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source group. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the inventory source group. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source group. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `inventory_source_group_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the inventory source group. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the inventory source group. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the inventory source group. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create inventory_source_group
inventory_source_group = provider.displayvideo_api.Inventory_source_group {
}

# Access inventory_source_group outputs
inventory_source_group_id = inventory_source_group.id
inventory_source_group_inventory_source_group_id = inventory_source_group.inventory_source_group_id
inventory_source_group_display_name = inventory_source_group.display_name
inventory_source_group_name = inventory_source_group.name
```

### Guaranteed_order

Creates a new guaranteed order. Returns the newly created guaranteed order if successful.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read ✅ Update

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `exchange` | String |  | Required. Immutable. The exchange where the guaranteed order originated. |
| `legacy_guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The legacy ID of the guaranteed order. Assigned by the original exchange. The legacy ID is unique within one exchange, but is not guaranteed to be unique across all guaranteed orders. This ID is used in SDF and UI. |
| `update_time` | String |  | Output only. The timestamp when the guaranteed order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String |  | Required. The display name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique identifier of the guaranteed order. The guaranteed order IDs have the format `{exchange}-{legacy_guaranteed_order_id}`. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the guaranteed order. |
| `publisher_name` | String |  | Required. The publisher name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `read_access_inherited` | bool |  | Whether all advertisers of read_write_partner_id have read access to the guaranteed order. Only applicable if read_write_partner_id is set. If True, overrides read_advertiser_ids. |
| `default_advertiser_id` | String |  | Output only. The ID of default advertiser of the guaranteed order. The default advertiser is either the read_write_advertiser_id or, if that is not set, the first advertiser listed in read_advertiser_ids. Otherwise, there is no default advertiser. |
| `read_write_advertiser_id` | String |  | The advertiser with read/write access to the guaranteed order. This is also the default advertiser of the guaranteed order. |
| `read_write_partner_id` | String |  | The partner with read/write access to the guaranteed order. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> |  | The IDs of advertisers with read access to the guaranteed order. This field must not include the advertiser assigned to read_write_advertiser_id if it is set. All advertisers in this field must belong to read_write_partner_id or the same partner as read_write_advertiser_id. |
| `default_campaign_id` | String |  | The ID of the default campaign that is assigned to the guaranteed order. The default campaign must belong to the default advertiser. |
| `status` | String |  | The status settings of the guaranteed order. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `exchange` | String | Required. Immutable. The exchange where the guaranteed order originated. |
| `legacy_guaranteed_order_id` | String | Output only. The legacy ID of the guaranteed order. Assigned by the original exchange. The legacy ID is unique within one exchange, but is not guaranteed to be unique across all guaranteed orders. This ID is used in SDF and UI. |
| `update_time` | String | Output only. The timestamp when the guaranteed order was last updated. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | Required. The display name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `guaranteed_order_id` | String | Output only. The unique identifier of the guaranteed order. The guaranteed order IDs have the format `{exchange}-{legacy_guaranteed_order_id}`. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the guaranteed order. |
| `publisher_name` | String | Required. The publisher name of the guaranteed order. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 240 bytes. |
| `read_access_inherited` | bool | Whether all advertisers of read_write_partner_id have read access to the guaranteed order. Only applicable if read_write_partner_id is set. If True, overrides read_advertiser_ids. |
| `default_advertiser_id` | String | Output only. The ID of default advertiser of the guaranteed order. The default advertiser is either the read_write_advertiser_id or, if that is not set, the first advertiser listed in read_advertiser_ids. Otherwise, there is no default advertiser. |
| `read_write_advertiser_id` | String | The advertiser with read/write access to the guaranteed order. This is also the default advertiser of the guaranteed order. |
| `read_write_partner_id` | String | The partner with read/write access to the guaranteed order. |
| `read_advertiser_ids` | Vec<String> | The IDs of advertisers with read access to the guaranteed order. This field must not include the advertiser assigned to read_write_advertiser_id if it is set. All advertisers in this field must belong to read_write_partner_id or the same partner as read_write_advertiser_id. |
| `default_campaign_id` | String | The ID of the default campaign that is assigned to the guaranteed order. The default campaign must belong to the default advertiser. |
| `status` | String | The status settings of the guaranteed order. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create guaranteed_order
guaranteed_order = provider.displayvideo_api.Guaranteed_order {
}

# Access guaranteed_order outputs
guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.id
guaranteed_order_exchange = guaranteed_order.exchange
guaranteed_order_legacy_guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.legacy_guaranteed_order_id
guaranteed_order_update_time = guaranteed_order.update_time
guaranteed_order_display_name = guaranteed_order.display_name
guaranteed_order_guaranteed_order_id = guaranteed_order.guaranteed_order_id
guaranteed_order_name = guaranteed_order.name
guaranteed_order_publisher_name = guaranteed_order.publisher_name
guaranteed_order_read_access_inherited = guaranteed_order.read_access_inherited
guaranteed_order_default_advertiser_id = guaranteed_order.default_advertiser_id
guaranteed_order_read_write_advertiser_id = guaranteed_order.read_write_advertiser_id
guaranteed_order_read_write_partner_id = guaranteed_order.read_write_partner_id
guaranteed_order_read_advertiser_ids = guaranteed_order.read_advertiser_ids
guaranteed_order_default_campaign_id = guaranteed_order.default_campaign_id
guaranteed_order_status = guaranteed_order.status
```

### Ad_group

Gets an ad group.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `ad_group_format` | String | The format of the ads in the ad group. |
| `line_item_id` | String | The unique ID of the line item that the ad group belongs to. |
| `product_feed_data` | String | The settings of the product feed in this ad group. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | The unique ID of the advertiser the ad group belongs to. |
| `ad_group_id` | String | The unique ID of the ad group. Assigned by the system. |
| `name` | String | The resource name of the ad group. |
| `entity_status` | String | Controls whether or not the ad group can spend its budget and bid on inventory. If the ad group's parent line item is not active, the ad group can't spend its budget even if its own status is `ENTITY_STATUS_ACTIVE`. |
| `targeting_expansion` | String | The [optimized targeting](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/12060859) settings of the ad group. |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the ad group. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. |
| `bid_strategy` | String | The bidding strategy used by the ad group. Only the youtubeAndPartnersBid field can be used in the bidding strategy. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access ad_group outputs
ad_group_id = ad_group.id
ad_group_ad_group_format = ad_group.ad_group_format
ad_group_line_item_id = ad_group.line_item_id
ad_group_product_feed_data = ad_group.product_feed_data
ad_group_advertiser_id = ad_group.advertiser_id
ad_group_ad_group_id = ad_group.ad_group_id
ad_group_name = ad_group.name
ad_group_entity_status = ad_group.entity_status
ad_group_targeting_expansion = ad_group.targeting_expansion
ad_group_display_name = ad_group.display_name
ad_group_bid_strategy = ad_group.bid_strategy
```

### Invoice

Lists invoices posted for an advertiser in a given month. Invoices generated by billing profiles with a "Partner" invoice level are not retrievable through this method.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `invoices` | Vec<String> | The list of invoices. This list will be absent if empty. |
| `next_page_token` | String | A token to retrieve the next page of results. Pass this value in the page_token field in the subsequent call to `ListInvoices` method to retrieve the next page of results. This token will be absent if there are no more invoices to return. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Access invoice outputs
invoice_id = invoice.id
invoice_invoices = invoice.invoices
invoice_next_page_token = invoice.next_page_token
```

### Ad_group_ad

Gets an ad group ad.

**Operations**: ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `non_skippable_ad` | String | Details of a [non-skippable short in-stream video ad](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216), between 6 and 15 seconds, used for reach marketing objectives. |
| `display_video_source_ad` | String | Details of an ad sourced from a Display & Video 360 creative. |
| `ad_group_ad_id` | String | The unique ID of the ad. Assigned by the system. |
| `display_name` | String | The display name of the ad. Must be UTF-8 encoded with a maximum size of 255 bytes. |
| `ad_urls` | Vec<String> | List of URLs used by the ad. |
| `ad_policy` | String | The policy approval status of the ad. |
| `entity_status` | String | The entity status of the ad. |
| `masthead_ad` | String | Details of an [ad served on the YouTube Home feed](//support.google.com/google-ads/answer/9709826). |
| `bumper_ad` | String | Details of a [non-skippable short video ad](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216), equal to or less than 6 seconds, used for reach. |
| `in_stream_ad` | String | Details of an [in-stream ad skippable after 5 seconds](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216), used for brand awareness or reach marketing objectives. |
| `ad_group_id` | String | The unique ID of the ad group that the ad belongs to. *Caution*: Parent ad groups for Demand Gen ads are not currently retrieveable using `advertisers.adGroups.list` or `advertisers.adGroups.get`. Demand Gen ads can be identified by the absence of the `ad_details` union field. |
| `audio_ad` | String | Details of an [audio ad](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216) used for reach marketing objectives. |
| `video_discover_ad` | String | Details of an [ad promoting a video](//support.google.com/displayvideo/answer/6274216) that shows in places of discovery. |
| `advertiser_id` | String | The unique ID of the advertiser the ad belongs to. |
| `name` | String | The resource name of the ad. |
| `video_performance_ad` | String | Details of an [ad used in a video action campaign](//support.google.com/google-ads/answer/10147229) to drive actions to the business, service or product. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl

# Initialize provider

    project = "my-project-id"
}

ad_group_ad_display_video_source_ad = ad_group_ad.display_video_source_ad
ad_group_ad_ad_group_ad_id = ad_group_ad.ad_group_ad_id
ad_group_ad_display_name = ad_group_ad.display_name
ad_group_ad_ad_urls = ad_group_ad.ad_urls
ad_group_ad_ad_policy = ad_group_ad.ad_policy
ad_group_ad_entity_status = ad_group_ad.entity_status
ad_group_ad_masthead_ad = ad_group_ad.masthead_ad
ad_group_ad_bumper_ad = ad_group_ad.bumper_ad
ad_group_ad_in_stream_ad = ad_group_ad.in_stream_ad
ad_group_ad_ad_group_id = ad_group_ad.ad_group_id
ad_group_ad_audio_ad = ad_group_ad.audio_ad
ad_group_ad_video_discover_ad = ad_group_ad.video_discover_ad

### Script

Creates a new custom bidding script. Returns the newly created script if successful. Requests creating a custom bidding script under an algorithm assigned to a line item will return an error.

**Operations**: ✅ Create ✅ Read

#### Fields

| Field | Type | Required | Description |
|-------|------|----------|-------------|
| `custom_bidding_script_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding script. |
| `errors` | Vec<String> |  | Output only. Error details of a rejected custom bidding script. This field will only be populated when state is REJECTED. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String |  | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm the script belongs to. |
| `active` | bool |  | Output only. Whether the script is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `name` | String |  | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding script. |
| `script` | String |  | The reference to the uploaded script file. |
| `create_time` | String |  | Output only. The time when the script was created. |
| `state` | String |  | Output only. The state of the custom bidding script. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | ✅ | Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the script. |


#### Outputs

| Output | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `custom_bidding_script_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding script. |
| `errors` | Vec<String> | Output only. Error details of a rejected custom bidding script. This field will only be populated when state is REJECTED. |
| `custom_bidding_algorithm_id` | String | Output only. The unique ID of the custom bidding algorithm the script belongs to. |
| `active` | bool | Output only. Whether the script is currently being used for scoring by the parent algorithm. |
| `name` | String | Output only. The resource name of the custom bidding script. |
| `script` | String | The reference to the uploaded script file. |
| `create_time` | String | Output only. The time when the script was created. |
| `state` | String | Output only. The state of the custom bidding script. |


#### Usage Example

```kcl
# main.k
import gcp

# Initialize provider
provider = gcp.GcpProvider {
    project = "my-project-id"
}

# Create script
script = provider.displayvideo_api.Script {
    custom_bidding_algorithm_id = "value"  # Required. The ID of the custom bidding algorithm that owns the script.
}

# Access script outputs
script_id = script.id
script_custom_bidding_script_id = script.custom_bidding_script_id
script_errors = script.errors
script_custom_bidding_algorithm_id = script.custom_bidding_algorithm_id
script_active = script.active
script_name = script.name
script_script = script.script
script_create_time = script.create_time
script_state = script.state
```
